Chapter 1125: Chapter 1124 Continuous Visits

"What, has Junior Brother Lu Yang reached the Transcendance Tribulation Stage now?"

"Isn’t the limit of the Void Refinement Stage the Body Integration Realm?"

"I don’t know."

Disciples of the Seek Dao Sect were agitated once again, even Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi displayed extremely surprised expressions, as even during their Void Refinement phase, they had never encountered such a situation.

Yingtian Immortal rarely fell silent for a moment.

Ever since he had met Lu Yang, this lad always stumbled upon unexpected situations, just like an Immortal Fairy whose motives were inscrutable.

Truly worthy of being from the Immortal Lineage.

Yingtian Immortal carefully sensed Lu Yang’s realm and, indeed, he was at the Transcendance Tribulation Stage.

"Venerable Immortal?" Lu Yang looked at Yingtian Immortal expectantly. He wasn’t picking a quarrel; he genuinely wanted to know what the issue was.

Yingtian Immortal pondered for a moment, his voice calm and unhurried, as if Lu Yang’s situation had been within his expectations all along.

"As the saying goes, every drink and morsel are preordained. You have surpassed your predecessors, passing the triple-layered Heavenly Tribulation deemed impossible, accomplishing an unprecedented feat and thus breaking through the ultimate limit of the Void Refinement Stage. This situation is an opportunity bestowed by me, on behalf of Heaven."

Lu Yang translated for Yingtian Immortal: The force of the Heavenly Tribulation was so strong it brought about a new situation.

This was almost what Lu Yang had guessed since Old Meng had also reached the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, although he slipped back down pretty quickly.

Although it was a new situation, it was a good one. According to ancient legends passed down, the sages who created the realm of Void Refinement did so in the hope that cultivators would get accustomed to subsequent realms in advance, thereby creating a new realm.

Being able to experience the power of the Transcendance Tribulation Stage during the Void Refinement Stage means that once we truly reach the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, cultivation will be twice as efficient with half the effort.

"Did you hear what Ying Tian Immortal Venerable said? The two Junior Brothers have encountered a fortuitous fairy encounter!"

To pass the test of immortals, to have an immortal reveal themselves, to obtain a fairy’s fortune, this would be a glorious tale to be passed down through the ages in any era.

"Is that really so?" Yun Zhi raised an eyebrow.

When she faced the Qian Heaven Thunder Tribulation during her tribulation, she felt that there was still potential to be tapped into within the Void Refinement Stage, but unfortunately, she could not control the thunder, and could not prove her conjecture. The changes in the little junior brother and Junior Brother Meng this time confirmed her thoughts.

"Little Yang, see what Immortal said? The harsher the tribulation, the greater the reward!"

Lu Yang had successfully passed his tribulation and had undergone a new transformation. Immortal Fairy seemed even more overjoyed than Lu Yang himself.

Looking at the exuberant Immortal Fairy and then at Qinghe, who was standing beside her showing no emotion, Lu Yang revealed a peculiar expression.

Fairy, you don’t seem like you’ve just woken up at all.

Considering it, it made sense. With such commotion from his tribulation, even if Fairy was hibernating, she would have woken up. How could she still be asleep?

So, does that mean Qinghe blocking me outside the Imperial Palace was actually on Fairy’s orders?

Lu Yangxin shivered within. As the saying goes, keeping company with the emperor is like accompanying a tiger. Was his Majesty’s action meant to sow discord between himself, a loyal minister, and the treacherous historian, thereby balancing the court relationships? Was this the art of an emperor’s mind?

Noticing that Little Yang’s gaze towards her was somewhat off, as if poking through her little scheme, Immortal Fairy smiled awkwardly.

She knew the principle that the greater the intensity of the tribulation, the greater the reward. Yet, seeing Little Yang struggling pitifully under the Heavenly Tribulation, she couldn’t bear to see him tormented, and worried that Little Yang would come seeking help, which would soften her resolve. Therefore, she had Little Lotus intervene.

Qinghe, whose hands were placed before her, stood silently as though she were a statue, contemplating nothing.

As an immortal descending upon the mortal world, she couldn’t appear for too long, as immortals must always maintain a sense of mystery and limit the time spent interacting with mortals.

Yingtian Immortal, who proposed this theory, naturally implemented his own philosophy.

"Today’s achievement is but a small step on the path of cultivation, do not take your practice lightly."

"I should not intervene too much in the affairs of the mortal world, take good care of yourselves."

"Yes!" Lu Yang and the other called out in unison.

A gentle breeze emerged from beneath, inflating Ying Tian Immortal’s dragon robe. The golden dragons embroidered on the robe blinked, moved about the fabric, then flew out of the garment to greet the wind, rapidly transforming into a divine dragon of immense size, drawing gasps of amazement from the onlookers.

The presence of the divine dragon exerted a subtle pressure, not intentionally so, but rather it was so immense that controlling it completely was difficult, allowing a tiny fraction to seep through.

Even this slight pressure gave everyone a sense of ancientness from a bygone era.

The divine dragon lowered its proud head. There is only one in the world who could make it bow—its master, the Ying Tian Immortal.

Ying Tian Immortal stood upon the dragon’s head, riding it back to the heavens, vanishing into the sky.

As Ying Tian Immortal disappeared, the dark clouds finally cleared, revealing the long-missed sunshine that warmed everyone pleasantly.

"Brother Ying Tian’s entrances and exits are always so distinct," Ao Ling couldn’t help but laugh and cry at the same time. He had never seen this divine dragon before; could it be that it was newly cultivated recently?

"It’s finally over!"

Lu Yang grimaced, passing through a tribulation was truly no easy task, and the pain was indeed real.

Despite the fact that the heavenly dew could heal injuries, both of them had not fully recovered yet, with wounds inside and out causing excruciating pain at the slightest movement. They would need at least a month of rest to recuperate.

"See, I didn’t lie to you, the greater the power of the tribulation, the greater the reward. I did all this for your own good."

"Get lost, it’s clear you didn’t predict this change at all!" freeωebnovēl.c૦m

As heroes who created history, both were surrounded by Disciples of Dao Seeking Sect and escorted to their respective beds to rest and heal comfortably.

"Little Yang, I need to step away for a moment," Fairy Eternity said.

"Ah, okay," Lu Yang replied without much thought, simply acknowledging her.

...

"Master, have you finished your business here?" Startling Swan found that ever since her master returned, the smile on his face never ceased, even more exaggerated than when he had left.

Since becoming a disciple, Startling Swan had never seen her master smile like this.

News spreads at its own pace, and the affairs of Dao Seeking Sect had not yet reached the Laurel Fairy Palace.

"Now I feel comfortable."

Considering that smiling all the time did not help in maintaining an authoritative image, Ying Tian Immortal turned his back to Startling Swan, enigmatic as ever.

Making an entrance observed by all, announcing to the world his return, and then departing on a dragon amidst the adoring gazes of the crowd—the sequence of events felt like a return to the awe-inspiring days of Ancient Times.

After suppressing it for three hundred thousand years, he finally regained that feeling.

Behind Ying Tian Immortal, the voice of a surprised Startling Swan rang out, "Eh, Immortal Fairy, how come you are here?"

"Young girl, leave us for a moment."

"Oh."

"Ying Tian, who allowed you to strike so fiercely!" Immortal Fairy stormed in, angrily seeking an explanation from Ying Tian Immortal.

Ying Tian Immortal turned around, looking at Immortal Fairy as if he had seen a ghost: "When I said I wanted the strike to be stronger, you agreed!"

"So what if I agreed?"

"Aren’t you being reasonable... hey, hey, hey, don’t self-detonate..."

Boom—

After the intense explosion, Immortal Fairy vanished without a trace, leaving only Ying Tian Immortal with a stunned expression.

Suddenly, space twisted again, and another visitor arrived to see Ying Tian Immortal.

"Come on, Daoist Yun Zhi, you don’t even say hello before you start swinging..."

Chapter 1126: Chapter 1125: Is There No Concept of Convalescence in Ancient Times?

"Senior Brother Lu Yang, you will get better."

"Junior Brother, everyone will remember you."

"Junior Brother Lu, you are the pride of our Seek Dao Sect!"

In the abode, lying on the bed with his hands crossed over his chest, Lu Yang was surrounded by fresh flowers and blessings, which was quite touching.

Whether it was senior brothers and sisters or junior brothers and sisters, having witnessed Lu Yang overcome the Heavenly Tribulation with his defying talents and receive blessings from an immortal to break through the limits of the Void Refinement Stage, they were greatly shocked. They then visited Lu Yang one after another to show their respect.

The new disciples, seeing their idol, couldn’t help but burst into tears.

There were too many people visiting Lu Yang, they spoke only a word to him, placed down flowers, and left to give time to those who followed.

"All right, time’s almost up, the second-in-command should rest."

Yun Mengmeng came out to take charge, hanging a ’No Visitation’ sign at the entrance of the abode.

After the guests left, Ao Ling and others, who didn’t know from where, appeared one after another, all coming to help take care of Lu Yang.

Even if they could not take care, having a lively atmosphere was excellent.

Lu Yang really wanted to ask, didn’t you have the concept of convalescence in Ancient Times?

Yun Mengmeng, seeing the flowers piled up several layers around Lu Yang and recalling that weaving flower wreaths was a custom in the Secret Realm to represent blessings, said,

"With so many flowers here, why not weave a big flower wreath to give a huge blessing to the second-in-command?"

Hearing this, Lu Yang quickly tried to divert Yun Mengmeng’s idea, "Sister Mengmeng, why not make flower cakes instead?"

"Did you like eating flower cakes, second-in-command?"

"Yes."

"I’ll go make them right away!"

Yun Mengmeng, holding several bunches of flowers, left.

These flowers were not only beautiful but also had high medicinal value; making them into flower cakes could also be considered a form of dietary therapy.

"It’s surprising, the changes one can undergo in the Void Refinement Stage."

Ao Ling and others circled around Lu Yang, clicking their tongues in wonder. In their time, there were no Heavenly Tribulations in the Void Refinement Stage; only from the Body Integration Realm to the Transcendance Tribulation Stage did such tribulations exist. The present Heavenly Tribulations were invented by the Yingtian Immortal after she became an immortal.

Now they couldn’t return to the Void Refinement Stage; they could only gather around Lu Yang to see the rarity.

"Not to mention, Senior Brother Lu has deep blessings, not only did he revive Immortal Sister, but he also received such great fortunes."

Lu Yang now only hoped that Immortal Fairy would come back soon to divert these people’s attention from studying him.

Eldest Senior Sister also was nowhere to be found.

"Two sisters, Sister Caiwei, it’s time to eat the Spirit Fruit." Qinghe came holding the freshly arranged spirit fruits.

When Immortal Fairy was not in the Spiritual Space, Qinghe used to reincarnate and didn’t stay in the Spiritual Space.

"And Lu Zhuguo, this is yours." Qinghe placed a plate of spirit fruits beside Lu Yang’s bed.

Lu Yang’s eyes twitched; this was the first time he had been addressed that way.

Lu Yang noticed the varieties of spirit fruits on the plate were different, but Qinghe had cut them into uniformly sized round shapes with silly smiling faces.

... These all looked suspiciously like an immortal.

Lu Yang ate a piece of spirit fruit, which was very sweet and made his throat feel much better; this piece must have had a lung-moistening function.

"But why is there no spiritual energy?"

Since they were spirit fruits, why was there no spiritual energy at all?

Qinghe sighed, patiently explaining, "Please understand your condition, Lu Zhuguo. You are currently in the Void Refinement Stage, with an unstable realm—one moment you could be in the Late Tribulation Stage and the next in the Early Stage of Qi Refinement."

"If you were in the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, naturally you could consume any level of spirit fruit, but if you were in the Early Stage of Qi Refinement, consuming spirit fruits would be a death wish."

"So everything you eat now can’t contain spiritual essence, to avoid harming your body further."

What she didn’t mention was that before bringing the spirit fruits in, she had advised Yun Mengmeng, who was pondering over making flower cakes, to bake out the spiritual essence from the flowers.

Lu Yang hadn’t expected there to be so much to consider.

"Little Lotus is truly as meticulous as ever," Jiang Lianyi said with a smile, teasing her. "No wonder Immortal Sister loves being looked after by you."

"You flatter me, Sister Lianyi, this is my only strength."

"There you go being modest again." Immortal Fairy triumphantly returned, entering through the grand doors of the abode.

"I’ve always said you’re great in every way; you just lack confidence."

"I still fall short compared to an adult."

"There you go saying that again."

"Is the Fairy back?" Lu Yang greeted from the bed.

"Yes, I just went to catch up with Ying Tian Immortal," said Immortal Fairy with a grin, pride written all over her face.

"Do you know where Eldest Senior Sister went?" Lu Yang had just asked Yun Mengmeng, and even she didn’t know where Eldest Senior Sister had gone.

"Miss Yun? I haven’t seen her." Immortal Fairy furrowed her brow, slightly surprised. Little Yang was injured and in bed, where could Miss Yun possibly be at a time like this?

"Forget it, Miss Yun won’t get into trouble. By the way, Little Yang, since you need to heal, let Little Lotus look after you."

"Cough, cough, cough—" Lu Yang suddenly started coughing violently, nearly coughing up internal injuries. What qualifications did he have to be looked after by a Semi-Immortal?

Lu Yang frantically signaled to Qinghe with his eyes, urging her to quickly reject Immortal Fairy’s absurd idea. Didn’t you always prefer taking care of the Fairy?

However, Qinghe completely ignored Lu Yang’s signals and seriously said, "I will follow the adult’s orders completely."

Lu Yang was dumbfounded; Qinghe, you’re really too stubborn.

"With Little Lotus looking after me, I can rest easy! So tired, so tired, I’m going to sleep."

Immortal Fairy stretched lazily and swiftly lay back on the grand bed in her Spiritual Space.

"Young Sect Master, would you like to see a Dream Mirage?"

Jin Caiwei held out a Recording Orb, which she had tested repeatedly. Finally, she managed to perfectly integrate the Dream Mirage with the Recording Orb, achieving an immersive effect.

No one else had yet seen her research results, and Lu Yang was the first one.

"Let’s see."

Lu Yang was interested, wanting to know if it was as he had imagined.

Jin Caiwei placed the Recording Orb on the ground, channeled a thread of spiritual essence into it, and the orb projected a light screen. It opened up like a realm, enveloping everyone and presenting a grand battle.

It was a Golden Phoenix rebirthing from Nirvana, her opponent a massive creature as red as the blazing sun, with six legs and four wings.

"Is this the fight Elder Lianyi had with Nation Master Zhu?" Lu Yang recognized the combatants instantly—it was the battle that founded the Demon Nation.

Although he had watched it in person, seeing a battle of Semi-Immortals twice definitely had its benefits.

Lu Yang felt as if he were really there, back in the Demon Nation—the effect of the Recording Orb was even better than he had imagined.

"Look at what you are doing; you should have used fire here!"

"And here, you hit too lightly." Ao Ling commented right in front of the persons involved, causing dissatisfaction.

"How dare you critique? You should know that today’s Zhu Tian isn’t the Zhu Tian from Ancient Times. He has countless Tribulation Crossing Demons under him; I’m the only one who can definitely beat him. If it were you, you probably couldn’t!"

"Ridiculous, what does having Tribulation Crossing Demons amount to? Are they going to defy heaven?" Ao Ling scoffed coldly.

Cold sweat broke out on Lu Yang; if this kept up, Elder Ao Ling might just challenge Zhu Tian to a fight.

"Junior Brother, are you okay?" Eldest Senior Sister arrived belatedly.

"Eldest Senior Sister!" Lu Yang felt her timing couldn’t be more perfect; she had saved the Demon Nation.

Eldest Senior Sister gently prodded Lu Yang’s injured spot.

"Does it hurt?"

"It hurts."

"That’s good. I just asked Chasing Moon True Person, and he said we could use the Seven Emotions Dao Fruit Embryo to convert your pain into pleasure. Should I ask for his help?"

Chapter 1127: Chapter 1126 Lu Yang: I Did My Best

Hearing the proposal from Eldest Senior Sister, Lu Yang was quite tempted.

Back when he was cultivating on Eldest Senior Sister’s Golden Core Star, the Jinwu Qi had refined him using the Seven Emotions Dao Fruit Embryo, and the effect was unexpectedly good.

He couldn’t feel any pain at all; it was truly joyful cultivation.

However, he still had concerns.

"Did Old Meng agree?"

Both he and Old Meng were recuperating. If Old Meng stubbornly insisted that it didn’t hurt and he didn’t need help from Chasing Moon True Person, then he couldn’t seek help from Chasing Moon True Person either!

"He agreed."

"I’ll go."

Eldest Senior Sister nodded, then disappeared, and the crowd hurriedly constructed a stretcher, lifting Lu Yang onto it.

"Ouch, it really hurts."

Meng Jingzhou was also surrounded by bouquets and well-wishes, creating a touching scene.

When people were around, Meng Jingzhou endured the pain and said it didn’t hurt, but as soon as everyone left, he started shouting out in pain.

The gains from Passing Tribulation were truly significant, and so was the pain.

"Junior Brother Meng, how are your injuries?" Eldest Senior Sister appeared in Meng Jingzhou’s abode.

Compared to Lu Yang’s noisy surroundings, Meng Jingzhou’s abode was much quieter, fitting for convalescence.

Seeing Eldest Senior Sister visiting him, Meng Jingzhou was quite moved and tried to struggle to his feet, but found his physical condition didn’t allow it, and could only lie in bed, "It’s alright, I need to rest quietly, and emotionally, I also need to avoid major fluctuations."

"I just asked Chasing Moon True Person, she said she could use the Seven Emotions Dao Fruit Embryo to turn your and your Junior Brother’s pain into joy. Shall I ask her to help?"

Meng Jingzhou didn’t answer right away but remained silent, seemingly hesitant about something.

"Junior Brother agreed."

"I’ll go!"

On Great Snow Mountain, two groups of people set off for the summit simultaneously.

Old Ma chewed on dried grass in his mouth, with several ropes tied to the saddle, and at the other end of the ropes was Meng Jingzhou lying on a rush mat.

Meng Jingzhou, lying on the mat looking at the sky, heard Lu Yang greet him, "Old Meng, how are you feeling?"

Meng Jingzhou turned his head and nearly burst a blood vessel.

Yun Mengmeng was leading the way in front, while Lu Yang lay on a stretcher, with Qinghe, Ao Ling, Jiang Lianyi, and Jin Caiwei each holding a corner of the stretcher, a rather luxurious assembly.

It’s not even something Emperor Xia could enjoy if he were severely injured—let alone his funeral!

Facing Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou remained unflustered, "It’s okay; I’ve been researching the Four Ancient Immortals lately and found out that besides Qilin Immortal who got married, the other three Immortals remain unmarried, suggesting that if one wishes to become an Immortal, it’s best not to involve oneself in romantic affairs."

"Gone soft?"

"You’re the one who’s gone soft!" Meng Jingzhou snapped angrily.

The two argued all the way from the foot to the top of the mountain until they saw Chasing Moon True Person and finally quieted down.

Chasing Moon True Person circled around them, "Rare indeed! Even the Yingtian Immortal disappeared for 300,000 years, and you two managed to alarm him with your tribulations."

Lu Yang thought to himself that it was no big deal; if the True Person were to return, perhaps she could also find the Yingtian Immortal at Laurel Fairy Palace.

"Pain turned into joy, is it? Easy."

Chasing Moon True Person activated the Seven Emotions Dao Fruit Embryo, and two red halos appeared in her palm, slapping them onto both individuals.

Lu Yang, originally aching all over, suddenly lit up his eyes and felt comfortable, the effect was immediate.

It was Meng Jingzhou’s first time enjoying this treatment, and his reaction was even greater than Lu Yang’s, "So comfortable!"

Although the injury had not changed, the healing process had become quite comfortable!

Suddenly, Meng Jingzhou’s expression froze, something was off.

"Old Meng, what’s wrong?"

Meng Jingzhou’s expression was weird as he transmitted to Lu Yang, "I was always tormented by lustful fire and felt very painful, but now I feel so comfortable."

"?"

Lu Yang worried that one day a good brother would really become a eunuch.

With Chasing Moon True Person’s wonderful rejuvenation, both good brothers returned to their respective abodes with peace of mind.

Lu Yang continued to lie in bed, watching the battle between the two Semi-Immortal Great Powers, Zhu Tian and Jiang Lianyi, with Qinghe feeding him fruit on the left, Yun Mengmeng feeding him small pieces of flower cake on the right, and also listening to Ao Ling, the foremost person below the Immortals, comment on the battle.

"See, your move was too slow, you can’t fight like this."

"This is a combat strategy I developed called static-quelling dynamics," retorted Jiang Lianyi.

Ao Ling smirked, as if saying she knew her too well, "Come on, that excuse might fool Senior Brother Lu, but you just woke up and your body is still sluggish, your reaction was half a beat slow."

Before this battle took place, Jiang Lianyi was using the Heaven-Deceiving Life-Defying Technique to sleep since ancient times and was accidentally found by Lu Yang, then awakened by Immortal Fairy.

"And this move, all flashy but clearly more powerful when in human form, yet you insisted on fighting in a phoenix form for the sake of appearance."

"And more..."

The more Jiang Lianyi listened, the redder her face got, and she had no rebuttal because Ao Ling was right.

But Jiang Lianyi couldn’t show weakness in front of Ao Ling, and with a stiff neck, she said:

"Don’t just talk the talk without walking the walk. See, among the Semi-Immortals, I’m the only one who can beat Zhu Tian, you really can’t, but if you don’t believe it, go and try!"

"How ridiculous, let’s try then!"

Lu Yang broke into a cold sweat listening to this—why had they started arguing again all of a sudden? Where was Eldest Senior Sister to save the day, and Senior Caiwei? Stop showing this battle, is there nothing else in the Recording Orb? Change it.

"A moment, esteemed predecessors, may I make a suggestion?" Lu Yang was genuinely worried that these two would end up seeking out Zhu Tian, bringing misery upon him.

Eldest Senior Sister was nowhere in sight, and Jin Caiwei didn’t change the content, leaving Lu Yang no choice but to step in and mediate.

Lu Yang held significant respect in the hearts of the two women; once he spoke up, they stopped arguing.

"This Demon Nation is, after all, part of our Great Bean Dynasty, and Nation Master Zhu handles the state affairs of the Demon Nation daily, which is very busy. When I met him in Demon City before, I told him that given his busy schedule, there was no need to come see me."

"If Ao Ling Senior were to seek out Nation Master Zhu, I fear it would disrupt the operations of the Demon Nation."

"Moreover, the strength of Ao Ling Senior is undoubtedly great and well-known, there’s no need to prove oneself over such matters."

After thinking it through, Ao Ling realized this was sound reasoning. Although Zhu Tian was not technically a member of the Great Bean Dynasty, he was fundamentally working for it. He shouldn’t fall for any provocation that could waste Zhu Tian’s time.

Seeing Ao Ling give up, Lu Yang quietly breathed a sigh of relief; the crisis had passed.

Jin Caiwei, squatting nearby, listened with great interest. Although she was at the Semi-Immortal level, she lacked battle experience and couldn’t spot any flaws in the fight, so listening to Sister Ao Ling’s analysis, she gained even more than Lu Yang.

"Knock, knock—"

"Is someone knocking?" Jin Caiwei saw the two sisters arguing, with Yun Mengmeng and Sister Qinghe feeding the Young Sect Master, leaving herself idle. So, she went to open the door.

Seeing the visitor, Jin Caiwei was quite surprised.

"Uncle Zhu Tian?"

Upon hearing Jin Caiwei’s voice, everyone looked towards the abode’s entrance.

There stood Zhu Tian at the entrance of the abode, accompanied by two Transcendence Tribulation Stage great demons.

Zhu Tian rubbed his hands together and grinned sheepishly: "I heard that Brother Lu Yang was injured, so I thought I’d stop by for a visit on my way."

Chapter 1128: Chapter 1127: A Bustling Abode

Lu Yang was stunned, never expecting Zhu Tian to come.

I just spent a lot of effort persuading Senior Ao Ling.

Zhu, I even let go of the issue of you sending me a beautiful woman, practicing virtue in return for grievances, don’t say I didn’t help, I really tried my best.

"What’s, what’s up?"

Zhu Tian asked cautiously, feeling that the atmosphere was somewhat off. Why was everyone staring at him—was it a wrong time for him to come?

He heard that Lu Yang had successfully passed the Transcendence Tribulation and even broke through the limits of the Void Refinement Stage, shocking the world.

But what he cared about was another matter—Brother Lu was injured.

The injury was definitely not severe, it wouldn’t be fatal nor leave any sequela, but since he was injured, that gave him a reason to visit and get closer.

After the battle in Demon City, he had been reflecting—every time something happened, Brother Lu was there. Was it a coincidence?

Although everyone had played their best cards, expended a huge amount of energy, and after a tough battle, still got defeated by Yun Zhi, they didn’t feel tired and appeared very spirited.

Before returning to the Abode, they had all lain on the ground and slept for a long time, now waking up and feeling mostly rested.

Their injuries were more serious than Lu Yang’s, but they had various methods to heal at an astonishing rate, and they were soon back in form.

In the blink of an eye, Emperor Dou personally led the troops, everyone marched grandiosely, leaving only Lu Yang alone in the empty house.

Lu Yang blinked his eyes, not understanding what they were up to.

He ate a piece of flower cake while drinking Enlightenment Tea, and realized something was wrong, quickly picking up a book to shake it.

"Oh no, crumbs fell into the crease of the book!"

When Lu Yang was engrossed in the Cultivation Technique, looking up a second time, he just caught the Great Bean Dynasty troops returning defeated.

"Failing fifteen times means nothing, everyone keep pushing..."

Watching everyone who did not forget to close the door softly before departing, Lu Yang absentmindedly ate a Spirit Fruit, suddenly making a grimace.

"So sour, what kind of Spirit Fruit is this?"

The third time he looked up, Fairy Eternity was once again motivating everyone:

"Failing eighty times means nothing, everyone take a break."

The people were so exhausted they staggered around, no longer having the strength to fight, even Qinghe simply collapsed on the ground from fatigue.

Even though they all were Semi-Immortals, they couldn’t withstand such repeated battles.

However, there were gains too, their combined tactics were advancing rapidly, the only problem was the enemy was too strong, their progress couldn’t be seen.

Lu Yang’s lips twitched, finally he couldn’t hold back and asked, "Fairy, what are you all doing?"

"Conquering strong enemies, extending territories!"

"Establishing unparalleled achievements, to be immortalized in Bean history!"

"Challenging oneself, breaking through limits!"

"Being honored as Marquis, reaching the pinnacle among officials!"

"One conquest forever, securing the land permanently!"

Everyone’s slogan reflected their own goals, Yun Mengmeng and others were shouting excitedly, seemingly not very tired.

The history of the Great Bean Dynasty’s battles was a history of tears and blood, with over eighty battles both big and small, not only did Emperor Dou personally lead the troops, all three Great Generals were mobilized, even the Historian and Minister of Rites who were civil officials had abandoned their pens to join the grim war.

Emperor Dou grieved for the hardships of the common people, regardless of how bad the battle situations were, he absolutely refused to tax them, not adding burdens to the common people, truly a wise ruler of his generation.

"We are fighting Miss Yun!" Fairy Eternity stated with hands on hips, head up as if engaging in something very remarkable.

Boom—

The doors of the Abode opened, the target of the conquest actively sought them out.

"Eldest Senior Sister!" Lu Yang raised his hands, honestly calling out to show he was innocent.

Yun Zhi glanced at the book on Lu Yang’s table, and the notes spread all over, nodded in satisfaction, "Fairy predecessor said you were compiling a Cultivation Technique, they didn’t want to disturb you at the Abode, so they went out to find some things to do. I’m just passing by to see if that’s really the case."

Lu Yang’s eyes twitched, Fairy, you guys might as well have stayed at the Abode playing cards or Mahjong.

"Well done, keep up the studying."

With a few words of encouragement, Yun Zhi prepared to leave, but was stopped by Lu Yang.

"Eldest Senior Sister, if I want to stabilize my realm, should I choose the path of living in peace or the path of fighting to sustain fighting?"

Yun Zhi thought about it and said, "Actually, it doesn’t really matter."

Lu Yang nodded, somewhat understanding Eldest Senior Sister’s point, "Eldest Senior Sister, you mean all roads lead to Rome, and no matter which one I choose, they essentially are the process of understanding one’s heart and validating it, aligning with my cultivation technique, right?"

"No, what I mean is, given your luck, even if you choose to live in peace, it will eventually turn into fighting to sustain."

"..."

Eldest Senior Sister, that makes me sad. Although I enjoy fighting, I never intentionally start conflicts. It is just that the Great Era’s conflicts have arrived, and battles are breaking out everywhere. I just inadvertently get dragged into them.

"Don’t be afraid, Little Yang. The Great Bean Dynasty will always be your strong backbone. Just go on and live in peace, and if you encounter any battles, we’ll fight them for you!" Fairy Eternity said with great loyalty.

The Great Bean Dynasty stood unyielding for years, growing larger and even establishing Crown Prince Lu Yang, all thanks to Fairy Eternity who did not care about abilities but only about close relationships, appointing people purely based on merit and harboring the spirit of brotherhood.

After Eldest Senior Sister left, Lu Yang sighed heavily, unsure of when Eldest Senior Sister would come to assist him and when this undercover identity would end.

In cultivation, there are no seasons. Lu Yang locked himself in his abode, studying tirelessly both day and night, while the rest of the Great Bean Dynasty folks locked themselves in his abode as well, playing around day and night.

Both parties had their own things to do, and the time passed peacefully.

"It’s about time," Lu Yang picked up a stack of paper and flicked it lightly.

These days, he researched cultivation techniques, gleaned meanings, peeled layers after layers, and combined with his understanding, he finally had a piece of work to show.

Then, with a bang, the papers turned to bits of dust.

Lu Yang covered his face. Just now, he had suddenly surged to the Early Tribulation Stage and couldn’t control his strength, reducing his work to ashes.

Luckily, it was his own work, and he could rewrite it quickly.

"I’ll go to Eldest Senior Sister."

Lu Yang had mostly recovered by now; he could walk without limping and didn’t need support.

He opened the entrance to his abode, and Fairy Eternity and others followed him like bodyguards.

Lu Yang found Eldest Senior Sister at the summit of Sky Gate Mountain, where she had been spending her time recently.

Eldest Senior Sister was sitting on the Emperor’s Chair, holding a book of sword techniques while Third Senior Sister blindly played the zither by her, the scenery picturesque as the wind rustled through the grass.

Seeing Lu Yang arrive, Yun Zhi subtly put away the book of sword techniques, but Yun Mengmeng still caught her.

"Ah, Xiao Zhi, you’re looking at the sword techniques again. Can’t you be like me, if you can’t learn it, just give it up?"

Yun Zhi pretended not to hear Yun Mengmeng’s comment, not stooping to argue with her bosom sister.

"Is the cultivation technique finished?"

"Yes."

Lu Yang respectfully handed the cultivation technique to Yun Zhi.

Yun Zhi looked it over and quietly uttered two words, "Not bad."

Compared to when he first started writing cultivation techniques, the junior brother had clearly made significant progress.

"Let me see, let me see."

Hearing Xiao Zhi praise the Second-in-command, Yun Mengmeng clamored to see it, and Ao Ling, Qinghe, and others also shoved their heads together to look at the cultivation technique in Yun Mengmeng’s hands.

"Indeed, not bad." Qinghe was surprised. Although there were a few flaws, those were based on her current perception. If it were her in the Void Refinement Stage, she definitely couldn’t possibly write such a level of cultivation technique.

"Young Sect Master is really impressive."

"Of course, how can our Second-in-command be anything but impressive?"

"Eldest Senior Sister, then this cultivation technique..." Lu Yang looked at Yun Zhi with anticipation.

"Only needs forty percent modification."

Chapter 1133: Chapter 1132: Mastering the [Rules]

Compared to the past when Eldest Senior Sister needed to significantly revise the cultivation techniques, this time she only had to make a forty percent revision, a clear sign of Lu Yang’s progress.

After composing these techniques for so long, he had finally passed.

"Sit down and rest for a while, I will correct it for you," Yun Zhi said, gesturing for Lu Yang not to stand.

Yun Zhi took out the Four Treasures of the Study, while Lu Yang stood beside her, grinding ink and passing the brush, learning how Eldest Senior Sister revised his cultivation techniques.

Lu Yang watched attentively as Fairy Eternity rested her head on Lu Yang’s shoulder, watching as well.

Elegant brushstrokes smeared and inscribed on the cultivation techniques, adding and deleting words and sentences, enhancing the content.

Lu Yang suddenly realized that as the Eldest Senior Sister, her vision was indeed higher than his; it seemed that he was far from capable of writing cultivation techniques on his own.

Yun Zhi blew on a stack of papers, drying the ink, "Done."

"Yay, Second-in-command’s cultivation technique is finally complete!" Yun Mengmeng cheered, somehow obtaining a handful of candy and distributing it among everyone to celebrate the hard-won achievement of Lu Yang’s technique.

The candy was wrapped in glutinous rice paper, ready to eat without removing the packaging.

Lu Yang tasted one, sweet with a hint of sourness, probably the flavor of a grape-like spirit fruit.

Yun Zhi’s candy was peach-flavored; although Yun Mengmeng had grown tired of peaches in the secret realm, Yun Zhi hadn’t.

"Alright, Little Yang’s matter is settled, let’s get to the real work!" Immortal Fairy once again rallied everyone for a full assault.

After eighty failures, they calmed their minds, refraining from rushing into battle and instead focusing on recovery. Now, with sufficient rest, and with Yun Zhi having completed Lu Yang’s cultivation technique—rendering him of no further use—the time to strike was now!

"Miss Yun, you mustn’t have anticipated our sudden attack. You’ve probably been on guard against us these past days, but certainly, you didn’t expect that we had no intention of attacking at all. Instead, we’ve been residing in Little Yang’s abode and just playing around. This is waiting for the rabbits to come to us!"

"It’s ’waiting at one’s ease for the exhausted enemy,’ Fairy." Although Lu Yang was indeed surprised on behalf of Eldest Senior Sister, he couldn’t help but correct her.

"Ah, right, that’s the phrase, Little Yang is correct! Charge!"

At the command of Immortal Fairy, all the women attacked at once.

The three Great Generals transformed into their original forms, a black Dragon, a fire Phoenix, and a white Tiger, majestically towering with teeth as tall as a person and shining white enough to reflect Yun Zhi’s shadow.

Had anyone harbored guilt in their hearts, the sight of these ancient Immortal Beasts would send them scrambling in terror.

Qinghe held a lotus flower, activating the Longevity Dao Fruit Embryo to slow time.

Yun Mengmeng imbued the clothing of everyone present with the power of the Initial Form of Immortal Dao Fruit, ensuring that the garments would not be damaged in battle.

Looking at the eager crowd, Yun Zhi held her forehead and sighed, instructing Senior Sister Gan Tian to tidy up things like the Emperor’s Chair to avoid damaging it.

Senior Sister Gan Tian moved adeptly. Initially surprised by the women challenging Eldest Senior Sister, she was now accustomed to it.

After putting everything away, Gan Tian continued to play the guqin, the tunes no longer soothing but filled with the vigor of armed combat.

Thud, thud, dong, dong—

Inspired by Gan Tian’s music, the women, brimming with fighting spirit, set up an Array Method to besiege Yun Zhi.

"Dragon and Phoenix Tiger Transformation!" This was the combined attack technique of the three Great Generals, subtly in line with the power of the three talents. Jiang Lianyi and Jin Caiwei turned into flat tattoos, adhering to Ao Ling’s body.

"Immortality!" Yun Mengmeng and Qinghe acted together, harnessing their closely-related Dao Fruit Outlines to create a realm where time nearly stood still.

This was the result of their eighty battles, allowing them to bridge the gap between mortals and Immortals, even challenging an Immortal in combat!

Soon, the women fell one by one to the ground, sleeping sweetly like dumplings into boiling water.

Yun Zhi, step by step, approached Lu Yang, radiating a murderous aura, with a field of slain sprawled out before them, causing Lu Yang to tremble with fear.

"Junior Brother, it’s time for you to return to your cultivation."

Lu Yang nodded like a pecking chick.

Fairy Eternity was still not convinced, "Hmph, Miss Yun, don’t be so proud. If I weren’t seriously injured and unable to condense my physical body, I would definitely challenge you to a duel!"

Yun Zhi’s cheeks twitched, pretending not to hear what was said.

Lu Yang stepped in to mediate, easing the tension between Eldest Senior Sister and Fairy Eternity, "His Majesty has personally taken to the battlefield, aiming to bolster the morale and spirit of the troops, truly a wise decision. However, the military is a tool of danger; war a perilous endeavor. Victory and defeat are common in military campaigns; it’s not just the victory that is precious, but the ability to withdraw and plan anew also does not diminish a hero’s true nature!"

Fairy Eternity pondered over Lu Yang’s words seriously, "Are you suggesting that this Immortal should retreat?"

"Yes."

"Oh, then let’s go back."

Fortunately, Yun Zhi understood the principle of not pursuing a defeated enemy too far. After their victory, she did not press for a complete annihilation, giving Lu Yang and the others ample time to withdraw. Lu Yang had no choice but to carry each of the women back to the Abode one by one.

The women were still sleeping and didn’t seem like they would wake up soon, so Lu Yang began to focus on studying the Cultivation Technique.

After cycling through the Grand Circulation with the new technique, Lu Yang felt his Realm slightly stabilize, which meant that even if he did nothing and continued to cultivate step by step, he would eventually be able to advance to the Body Integration Realm.

"However, the rate is rather slow."

"That’s quite normal. It means you haven’t grasped the essence of the Void Refinement Stage," Fairy Eternity floated leisurely around the Abode, her feet off the ground, like a ghost.

"Essence?"

"I ask you, what’s the biggest difference between the Void Refinement Stage and the Body Integration Realm?"

"Difference? Control of the Rule?"

"Right, controlling the Rule. The better your grasp of the Rule, the more stable your Realm will become."

"So that’s how it is, but how exactly do you control the Rule?" asked Lu Yang, the Emperor’s Master, unashamed to seek knowledge, as he was completely clueless about the Rule.

"You are currently at the verge of the Body Integration Realm, close your eyes and try to extend your Spiritual Power outward, to sense your Abode."

Taking advantage of the momentary stability of his Realm, Lu Yang released his Spiritual Power throughout the Abode. He could see every nook and cranny clearly, even the sight of the women sleeping peacefully, as well as the crumbs from the cookies they had dropped on the ground earlier.

"Next, imagine your body becoming ethereal, merging with the space of your Abode."

Imagination was one of Lu Yang’s strengths. He imagined himself as a pool of water, spreading in all directions, covering every inch of space as though his Abode had become part of his domain, subject to his whims.

Fairy Eternity’s teachings echoed in Lu Yang’s ears, "Lastly, and most importantly, words carry power. Each phrase you utter carries your strength."

"Now, establish a Rule within this space. Any Rule will do."

"I hereby establish the [Rule: within the Abode, all cookie crumbs must go into the trash can]."

As the Rule was established, the crumbs on the floor flew up and went straight into the trash can.

"Yes, yes, yes, that’s the idea!" Fairy Eternity didn’t expect Lu Yang to succeed on his first try.

Buoyed by his success, Lu Yang continued his cultivation, "I hereby establish the [Rule: within the Abode, books must dance]."

The books on the desk, borrowed from the Scripture Pavilion, stood up, their corners like legs, hopping and dancing on the table, defying common sense.

Lu Yang felt he was close to uncovering the trick. With such a genius act, the more spectators, the better.

"I hereby establish the [Rule: Yun Mengmeng, Qinghe, Ao Ling, Jiang Lianyi, Jin Caiwei wake up]!"

"Wait, you can’t set Rules for people with a higher Cultivation Level than you!" Fairy Eternity hastily said.

"Pfft!"

The moment the Rule was established, Lu Yang sensed something was wrong, a rush of blood surged upward, and he violently spat out a mouthful of blood.

The women had just opened their eyes to see Lu Yang lying on the ground, spewing blood like a fountain.

Chapter 1134: Chapter 1133: Disregarding Sword Immortal Lu’s Kind Intentions

"Senior Brother, are you all right?"

Lu Yang genuinely frightened all the girls, who were alarmed to find him seriously injured when they had just seen him perfectly fine before they went to sleep. How could he have suddenly sustained such heavy injuries?

Was he beaten by the Eldest Senior Sister?

The girls hurriedly carried Lu Yang to the bed.

"Cough cough, just a minor accident," he said.

Lu Yang had gotten too excited about mastering a rule and now, after spitting out a few mouthfuls of hot blood, he had calmed down. How could he even think of commanding five Semi-Immortals with a Body Integration Realm rule? That was practically courting death.

Indeed, one should never become too ecstatic.

Fortunately, the rule he had set was not the kind that twisted causality against the heavens, which merely woke the girls up. Otherwise, his injuries could have been worse than when he faced the Thunder Tribulation.

Despite the blood he was spitting out, influenced by the Seven Emotions Dao Fruit Embryo, Lu Yang felt rather comfortable.

No, no, this comfort was unacceptable. Lu Yang forced himself to stop.

He worried he might one day seek out pain for pleasure, such was the terrifying effect of the Seven Emotions Dao Fruit Embryo, changing his habits without a sound.

Knock knock.

The knocking on the door came, and Fairy Eternity slipped into the Spiritual Space in a flash, Jin Caiwei hurried to answer it, and Tao Yaoye was at the door.

"Elder Brother Lu Yang, how’s your injury?"

During the time Lu Yang was healing, Tao Yaoye had visited a few times. It wasn’t her first time seeing Yun Mengmeng and a room full of people guarding Lu Yang, but every time she felt like she was losing to them.

"Senior Brother, are you all right?"

Seeing the blood at the corner of Lu Yang’s mouth and the bedsheet soaked with blood, she was shocked. How had his injuries gotten so severe?

"There’s no need to worry, Junior Sister Tao," Lu Yang said in a nonchalant tone. "I just hit a snag while cultivating. It’s common to have such minor issues; I’ll just need to be more careful next time."

Since Lu Yang acted as if nothing were amiss, Tao Yaoye didn’t feel it appropriate to say much more.

"I come on behalf of Junior Brother Man to visit you. A few days ago, Junior Brother Man wanted to visit and say farewell in person, but at the time you were in seclusion, so he asked me to pass on his message before he left."

Those few days were when Lu Yang was in seclusion, studying and writing cultivation techniques, refusing all visitors. He had only just removed the "In Seclusion" sign not long ago.

"Does Junior Brother Man have some mission that requires him to travel far?" Lu Yang wondered. Was Man Gu going to be away for a long time, that he needed to say goodbye to him?

"No, he went to the Imperial City to take part in the Imperial Examination."

"Ah?"

"Junior Brother Man believes that the best way to achieve Enlightenment among the common folk is to join the Dynasty as an official and become a regional governor."

If he waited to break through to the Void Refinement Stage before taking the exams, it would be dangerous to even leave the house. He could only take the exams before the breakthrough.

"Although our Sect could recommend him for a position in the Dynasty, he prefers to become an official through his own scholarly achievements."

Considering Man Gu was slightly above Fairy Eternity in level, Lu Yang was quite worried about him.

On the contrary, Fairy Eternity had a lot of confidence in Man Gu: "Man Gu will definitely pass. He is the only one from the Ancient Barbarian Tribe and received a blessing from Immortal herself."

This only made Lu Yang more concerned.

After Tao Yaoye left a new Recording Orb and departed, Fairy Eternity finally emerged from the Spiritual Space.

"In fact, to master the rules, staying in Seek Dao Sect is not the best option."

Lu Yangxin’s heart stirred, and he thought of an excellent place, "Are you talking about Buddha Country?"

"Exactly, the best choice is Buddha Country. Mastering the rules is fundamentally about comprehending heaven and earth. With an Immortal Body in Buddha Country, the effect is even better than if you were to ascend to the Transcendance Tribulation Stage and comprehend heaven and earth!"

Given the opportunity to go to Buddha Country, Lu Yang had no reason to disagree.

He could finally be an Immortal again.

Before heading to Buddha Country, Lu Yang kindly asked his good brother Old Meng if he would like to accompany him.

Meng Jingzhou looked at Lu Yang and the five Semi-Immortals behind him then thought about Lu Yang becoming an Immortal in Buddha Country while he was still known as a Buddha’s son. If I go to Buddha Country, will I have a single day of peace?

Lu Yang earnestly advised Meng Jingzhou, implying only his well-being, "Old Meng, you should seize this chance for an Immortal fate. Once I’m in Buddha Country, I’ll be an Immortal, and you’ll have an Immortal brother. I’m happy for you just thinking about it."

"Get lost, get lost, get lost."

Meng Jingzhou disregarded Sword Immortal Lu’s kind intentions. Sword Immortal Lu couldn’t say much more, so he, along with Fairy Eternity, Yun Mengmeng, Qinghe, Ao Ling, Jiang Lianyi, and Jin Caiwei, set out alone for Buddha Country.

Theoretically, someone at the Void Refinement Stage should go out as little as possible. There were several days of travel from Seek Dao Sect to Buddha Country; however, with many Semi-Immortals accompanying him, there shouldn’t be any issues.

Apart from Lu Yang pulling out his sword to assist whenever he saw injustice on the road, saving a damsel in distress, and subsequently finding out it was for a Dream Mirage film, in which he accidentally appeared, the director hearing of Lu Yang’s appearance sincerely invited him to make a cameo in the Dream Mirage.

And accidentally entering a sealed-off small mountain village where a female ghost at the Consummation of Qi Refinement level died with grievances, killing passers-by and casting an illusory curse on Lu Yang, only to be slain by a strand of his hair. Further investigation by Lu Yang revealed that the man who killed the ghost had since become a prince consort, prompting Lu Yang to write a letter, hoping Emperor Xia would deal with it.

In order to avoid trouble and hide his identity, Lu Yang went to a barbecue restaurant again and discovered issues with customer deception and non-fresh ingredients, with a staff member even yelling at Lu Yang, saying, "What can you do about it?" Lu Yang immediately used a talisman to contact the Jiuyou Sect, asking them to focus on quality control while expanding and to deal with this staff member as they saw fit. Upon hearing this, the Sect Master of Jiuyou Sect personally hurried over, greeting Young Sect Master Lu with a line of trembling members, scaring the staff member out of his wits.

Only then did he safely reach Buddha Country.

"I always said Eldest Senior Sister was not good at judging people, look how well this worldly transformation worked out. There was no need to fuel wars through fighting." Lu Yang felt this journey was very peaceful; he wouldn’t have needed Yun Mengmeng and the others to protect him.

After arriving in Buddha Country, Lu Yang condensed his Immortal Body and, with the help of Fairy Eternity’s Immortal Sense, became an Immortal.

"This is much more comfortable," Lu Yang couldn’t help but sigh. There really was no better place than Buddha Country, they didn’t have such good days in Seek Dao Sect.

"This is Elder Brother Lu Yang’s Immortal Body." The ladies marveled. Except for Fairy Eternity and Qinghe, they had only heard about Lu Yang being able to condense an Immortal Body and had never truly seen it.

Today, they witnessed it and indeed found it miraculous.

...

Imperial City, Imperial Examination Hall.

Today is the day of the Imperial Examination, an event held every five years, gathering talented individuals from across the world to display their abilities in writing.

Just as the examination began, a student experienced a crisis, breaking out in profuse sweat and raising his hand to signal.

The invigilator walked over unhurriedly, "What’s the matter, candidate?"

The invigilator glanced at the candidate’s ID tag: Man Gu.

"I have an issue; may I leave the room temporarily?"

The invigilator frowned and reprimanded, looking askance at Man Gu: "Of course not. The examination lasts for three days, and during this period no candidate may leave. You want to leave as soon as the exam starts. Are you trying to pass on the questions to your accomplices?"

Such incidents had happened several times in the history of the examination.

Desperate and sweating profusely, Man Gu said, "But I really can’t hold it in."

"Eating, drinking, and relieving oneself must all be done here. No leaving is permitted!"

"It’s my Realm I can’t hold in."

Chapter 1135: Chapter 1134: Seeking Help Outside the Arena

The examiner’s expression changed drastically, no longer maintaining his previously light and breezy demeanor.

Among the candidates, there were not a few cultivators. To prevent the cultivators from cheating, the Imperial Examination Hall had set up a Spirit Extinguishing Array Formation, rendering all cultivator methods useless.

But what array method could withstand the descent of Heavenly Tribulation?

"You, you need to get out of here!"

"It’s too late." Man Gu’s forehead was slick with cold sweat as he looked up at the sky. In a flash, the weather changed, with lightning flashing and thunder roaring. The Heavenly Tribulation had locked on to Man Gu!

"Candidates, evacuate the examination area quickly!" the examiner shouted. Since Man Gu couldn’t leave, the candidates needed to get out fast. This was no joke—if the tribulation struck, few present could withstand it.

Having never seen such a spectacle before, the candidates panicked. Such a tribulation was what one faced when advancing from the Divinity Transformation Stage to the Void Refinement Stage. Whether the city they were in even had cultivators at the Divinity Transformation Stage was questionable, let alone having witnessed a Heavenly Tribulation.

The candidates hurriedly evacuated the examination area, leaving Man Gu behind alone.

Man Gu’s face went pale as he looked at the rolling thunder in the sky.

This was bad. The more people there were around during the transcending of the Heavenly Tribulation, the more powerful the tribulation became. Just now, the Heavenly Tribulation had not only locked onto him but also onto the tens of thousands of candidates, causing the power of the Thunder Tribulation to skyrocket far beyond his capability!

To say nothing of the fact that he was currently only at the Divinity Transformation Stage, even if he were at the Body Integration Realm, he couldn’t withstand it.

Moreover, it was too late for the candidates to escape. The Heavenly Tribulation regarded them all as factors affecting the transcendence and intended to strike them all down with thunder!

"This definitely won’t do!"

Gritting his teeth, Man Gu sacrificed his primordial spirit and clasped his hands together, muttering a prayer, "Immortal, please protect us. Man Gu humbly summons the mightiest ancestor of the Barbarian tribe!"

His primordial spirit could call upon the strength that the ancestors of the Barbarian tribe had left in this world.

Different from the last time he had summoned an ancestor of the Barbarian tribe when he had called upon the most powerful ancestor during the Divinity Transformation Stage in Ancient Times.

This time, he cast aside levels and called upon the absolute strongest of all the ancient Barbarian ancestors!

With a crack, the resplendent thunder descended, and the candidates could no longer control their fear, crouching down while holding their heads.

A slender figure tore through the void, striding forward to face the vicious onslaught of the Thunder Tribulation. A corner of his mouth curled up in a disdainful smile, and with a casual wave of his hand, he repelled the thunderous attack.

"Someone has repelled the Thunder Tribulation with one strike—who is this Great Power?!"

"I don’t recognize him."

"He just appeared out of thin air, what realm does a Great Power need to be in to do that?"

Both the candidates and the examiners buzzed with discussion but could not identify this figure with any known world-renowned powerhouse.

The strong ones in the Imperial City also noticed the commotion at the Imperial Examination Hall. In the dark, world-covered heavens and earth, they saw only that slender white figure courageously facing the Thunder Tribulation, standing unshaken, which was awe-inspiring.

The slender figure seemed like an Immortal King seated high in the nine heavens, indifferent to the world, disregarding the discussions of the candidates.

Lu Yangxin felt secretly pleased within his heart, thinking that it was the right time to arrive. Let everyone shout louder, even louder.

This was the meaning of cultivation, wasn’t it? If he didn’t show off in front of a crowd, what was the point of his cultivation?

Having just arrived in the Buddha Country to consolidate his Immortal Body, Lu Yangxin had felt someone calling out to him, similar to how Man Gu had called out to him before.

When Man Gu last summoned him, he had been caught off guard and was directly pulled over. Now that he was an Immortal, he, of course, couldn’t be pulled over directly.

However, if Man Gu was summoning him, there must be a reason. Lu Yangxin’s true form couldn’t leave the Buddha Country, so he could only split off a fraction of his power to help Man Gu, to see what was happening.

And he had encountered the Heavenly Tribulation upon arrival.

Although the Lu Yangxin who came to the Imperial City was just a clone, it was more than enough to deal with the Heavenly Tribulation, easily shattering it with a lift of his hand.

Man Gu was also stunned. Did he have such a powerful presence among his ancestors?

"Junior Brother Man, it’s me." Lu Yang sent a message to Man Gu. He wasn’t sure of the situation on Man Gu’s side, so he had disguised himself before coming.

"Brother Lu?!" Man Gu’s mouth dropped open in disbelief. Had Lu Yang become the strongest being in their Barbarian tribe?

Boom—

The second Thunder Tribulation followed swiftly, giving Lu Yang no chance to catch his breath.

Lu Yang soared into the sky above the Imperial City and with the Buddha Land in Palm, extended one finger, which was enormously huge, easily covering more than ten Imperial Examination Halls.

Lu Yang pointed to the Cave Heaven, letting the Thunder Tribulation strike his finger while casually chatting with Man Gu to understand the whole situation.

"So, you accidentally broke through your realm during the Imperial Examination," Lu Yang found the situation amusing. Many cultivators at the Spirit Transformation Stage spent their entire lives unable to find the opportunity to break through, yet Man Gu had to suppress his realm, a shame he couldn’t keep it under control.

"The Array Method in the examination hall suppressed the Spiritual Energy within my body, causing me to lose control over my realm," Man Gu exclaimed his innocence. He had originally planned to make a breakthrough in cultivation as a celebration after securing an official position.

"Let it be, since this was supposed to be your Heavenly Tribulation, you were bound to face it."

Lu Yang intercepted most of the Thunder Tribulation, allowing only a small portion to fall on Man Gu.

To breakthrough, one must be struck by lightning; this is a necessary part of the body tempering process and simply cannot be skipped.

Man Gu shouted out loud, invoking the bloodline of the Ancient Barbarian Tribe, enduring the explosions of lightning on his body that tore skin and flesh without uttering a cry of pain, upholding the name of the Ancient Barbarian Tribe.

Fairy Eternity floated out from the Spiritual Space, with Little Yang and Junior Brother Man both undergoing their Thunder Tribulation, she seemed to be the only one unoccupied.

"Let this Immortal see what this Imperial Examination tests," she mused.

"The way of the great learning lies in enhancing illustrious virtue, in loving the people, in stopping at the utmost good. Debate—what is the great learning?"

"Is it appropriate for the Prime Minister to summon wise talents from all directions for counsel and see guests for discussion in his private residence?"

"What do all these mean?"

Fairy Eternity scratched her head, feeling the questions were incomprehensible, even more difficult to understand than Little Yang’s words.

Chapter 1139: Chapter 1138 [Rule: Remove Things That Affect My Cultivation]

The Buddha worshipped at the Soybean Temple was a real Buddha!

In the Great Bean Dynasty, at the Ancestral Temple.

The echo of Lu Yang’s previous words reverberated in the temple, startling the eagle-eyed man and the Great Monk.

It turned out that when the Worldly Venerable uttered those words, he wasn’t addressing them, but rather the hunched elder.

To overlook the past and predict the future—is this a glimpse of the Venerate’s extraordinary power?

"Who is speaking!" The hunched elder’s skin crawled as he could not pinpoint the source of the voice.

Lu Yang extended a finger, placing it on the hunched elder’s forehead. The elder remained immovable.

In the elder’s eyes, that was not merely a finger, but rather the sky collapsing, smashing the temple and ruthlessly crushing him.

The monk was unwilling to reveal himself to the world, but seeing as three benefactors have entered the temple with a dispute, it was only right for the monk to intervene.

Could it be that the Worldly Venerable was not referring to the three of them, but rather to Yue Changhe and his paternal and maternal grandfathers?!

Chapter 1152: Chapter 1151: Buddha Says It’s Ineffable

Yue Changhe’s grandfather soon followed in his father’s footsteps; the two men stood side by side, motionless, like a pair of statues.

These two had blood on their hands, and the monk and the eagle-eyed man, receiving one each, captured them to settle the matters, making the journey worthwhile.

In that moment, Yue Changhe felt profoundly fortunate; he understood that his fate with the Worldly Venerable was complete. If the Worldly Venerable were to reveal anything further, it might damage his own destiny.

Having the Worldly Venerable enlighten him and handle his two major enemies was already an enormous stroke of fate; he dared not ask for more.

Chapter 1154: Chapter 1153: The 800 Disciples of Tiger Roar Sect

Chapter 1159: Chapter 1158: In a Tight Spot but Resolute

"Teacher Lu, isn’t real-life training a bit too dangerous?" A student asked, shivering as he raised his hand. They had come enthusiastically for class, only to be told by Teacher Lu to go kill Demon Beasts in the wild?

These were Demon Beasts! Even their parents would run upon seeing one, how could they possibly stand a chance?

"You’ve trained in Tiger Roar Fist for so long, it’s time to test your Cultivation achievements. Don’t worry, I won’t pick too strong opponents for you."

The students groaned, although there was the powerful Teacher Lu watching over them, what if something uncontrollable happened?

Teacher Lu didn’t care much about what the students were thinking; he continued walking ahead with the flag, and the students had no choice but to follow.

"We have wolf tracks here; it should be this direction!" Lu Yang crouched and confidently pointed at the blank snowfield, like a seasoned hunter.

"Teacher, there are no footprints here?"

"The footprints have been covered by the heavy snow, You’re still young, you can’t see them, but the teacher can see the footprints beneath the snow."

The students looked up to Lu Yang with admiration.

Lu Yang was pleased with the students’ reactions and led them in the direction of the Wolf Demon his Spiritual Sense had detected.

After walking an unknown distance, Lu Yang raised his hand in a fist to signal everyone to stop.

He pointed behind a huge rock nearby and said, "See that big rock? There’s a Wolf Demon behind it. According to my experience, it’s a second-level Qi Refinement Wolf Demon, one-eyed and lame on the left leg, abandoned by its pack."

Fang Zhige looked bewildered, Can experience really tell all that?

"You don’t have to fight with them, I’ll find you a Demon Beast from the Foundation Establishment Stage to deal with."

Fang Zhige took a few steps back in disbelief, staring at Lu Yang, who looked indifferent.

How could this be, how could Teacher Lu see through his true Cultivation Level, even the Golden Core Stage Master Murong couldn’t!

Could it be that Master Luo hadn’t been troubling him because Teacher Lu had dealt with Master Luo?

Thinking of this, Fang Zhige lowered his voice and sternly warned, "Teacher Lu, you shouldn’t stir this muddy water. Perhaps Master Luo isn’t a threat to you, but behind him is the endless bounty of the Ghost Killing Alliance, and above that is the Nine Ghosts Alliance. You’ll be facing relentless pursuit!"

Thinking that such a good teacher as Lu Doudou might face a life-threatening situation because of him made Fang Zhige extremely remorseful.

"Alright kid, don’t worry about it too much, go and fight your Demon Beast."

It was then that Fang Zhige suddenly realized his greatest problem, he was only at Great Perfection of Qi Refinement and had never fought a Demon Beast from the Foundation Establishment Stage.

His learned assassination techniques were useless against Demon Beasts.

"Walk north for about a mile, there you’ll find a snow fox at the Early Stage of Foundation Establishment, go fight it."

Lu Yang patted Fang Zhige on the back, urging him to hurry.

In the Spiritual Space, huge snowflakes fell like goose feathers, burying the Imperial Palace of the Great Bean Dynasty. The roof of the palace was indistinguishable, and it was snowing inside the palace too, covering everything from the ground to the throne.

Immortal Fairy, wearing a white wolf skin, leapt up and down in the snow, howling and waving its wolf claws. As soon as Lu Yang turned to ask a question, she pounced on him.

"What are you doing, Fairy?"

After Lu Yang staggered to his feet, he realized Immortal Fairy had draped him in an unknown Demon Beast’s fur while he wasn’t looking.

"This is Bei Skin."

"Isn’t there a proverb ’a collusion between wolves,’ which describes a very close relationship? Now, I am the wolf, and you are the Bei; our relationship is unbreakable!"

And now, with his own realm fluctuating towards Foundation Establishment, how could he possibly be a match for these Demon Rabbits?

He feared this would be his end.

If he perished, it was of little concern, but the children must not be harmed!

Gong Che and Shi Yi urged with tears in their eyes, choked up with emotion.

They had a sinking feeling that this farewell might be their last.

Lu Yang’s eyes turned blood red as he threw himself into battle with the Demon Rabbits.

He could only rely on himself now.

When facing Demon Beasts he had never crossed swords with before, one couldn’t be too careful!

These Demon Rabbits couldn’t beat him and they still called for reinforcements?

With his wooden sword activated, he swept through the bear group like a scythe through wheat, mercilessly harvesting them without even a whimper.

The wooden sword released a burst of Sword Qi and shattered, unable to be used again. Lu Yang had to continue taking out new small wooden swords from his Identity Jade.

Later, finding it too bothersome to fetch wooden swords this way, he dumped all the swords from the sack, using his intention to float them behind his back, creating a forest of wooden swords.

For the cities in the Extreme Northern Lands, a beast tide was a cataclysmic disaster. Not only because of the presence of several Great Demon Kings but also because the endless hordes of Demon Beasts made the Human race’s skin crawl.

But no matter how numerous, these Demon Beasts were no match for Lu Yang.

Lu Yang strolled leisurely through the beast tide, his fingers lightly hooking forward, sending the small wooden swords flying and felling swathes of Demon Beasts.

Shick—

Chapter 1162: Chapter 1161: Man-Made Beast Tide

The city gate guards looked at Lu Yang as if they had seen a ghost. The descriptions from the students suggested that Lu Yang faced a situation where death was almost certain. Could this be explained by having just enough life-saving measures?

Lu Yang returned to Muxue City, accompanied by the students, but his presence was out of sync with the tense atmosphere of the city.

As the beast tide approached, Muxue City prepared for war, all cultivators were conscripted.

Before entering the martial arts hall, Lu Yang told his classmates to go home, declaring that today’s extracurricular activity had been very successful.

The martial arts hall was empty. Lu Yang inquired nearby and learned that the City Lord had gathered all the cultivators in the city to combat the beast tide, and Murong Da Ye and the others, as cultivators, had all been summoned.

"Speaking of which, who exactly triggered this beast tide?"

Lu Yang lay on his bed, recalling the remnants of a beast taming technique within the bodies of the Four Great Demon Kings, and murmured to himself.

This meant that the beast tide was not the natural disaster outsiders believed it to be, but a genuine man-made calamity.

"Is it to overwhelm Muxue City with the beast tide?"

Controlling the Four Great Demon Kings with a beast taming technique, the practitioner must definitely be a Pass Tribulation Cultivator. For a Pass Tribulation Cultivator, destroying Muxue City would be an easy task.

"Do they not want to make a move personally, or is there another agenda?"

Suddenly, there was a commotion in the martial arts hall.

"Did you see Vice City Lord Ma’s expression? Laughable, I thought he could only scowl, turns out he has other faces too."

"Alright, alright, keep your voices down. If Vice City Lord Ma’s people hear us, we’re finished."

When Lu Yang went outside, it turned out Sect Leader Murong Da Ye and his disciples had returned.

"Little Lu, you’re okay? I heard you took the kids outside the city to hunt demons and scared me to death," Murong Da Ye said with concern.

"Just lucky, didn’t encounter any powerful demon beasts."

"Hey, that’s why I say your luck isn’t just bragging; it’s real good. When you went out, the beast tide struck; had you encountered it, it would have been the end."

"Yeah, yeah, it was a city-destroying level beast tide. Even the City Lord had no answers," the inner sect disciples chattered, having encountered the legendary beast tide for the first time in their lives.

Lu Yang remained silent with a smile.

"I heard from a neighbor that you all were called by the City Lord to deal with the beast tide?"

"Exactly, I thought I was almost gone for good this time," Murong Da Ye said, still shaken, slapping his thigh.

"Don’t worry, sit down and take it easy," Lu Yang said smilingly, getting things organized. "I caught a few wild rabbits outside the city, let’s roast and eat them together."

"Ah, that’s wonderful," Murong Da Ye beamed with joy, his disciples also thrilled. In the barren Extreme Northern Lands, having a barbecue was one of the few forms of entertainment.

Lu Yang expertly set up the grill and listened to Murong Da Ye tell stories as he roasted the meat.

"At first, when Vice City Lord Ma summoned us, we were very scared. After all, it’s a beast tide. What could we, who are just at the stages of Qi Refinement, Foundation Establishment, and Golden Core, do? We were clearly going to our deaths."

"That Ma fellow even feigned concern, saying it was all for the continuation of Muxue City, asking us to hand over our cultivation resources for centralized allocation. If he’s so capable, let him charge at the beast tide first. It’s all nonsense, I think he just wanted to embezzle things. If the city were breached, he’d be the first to grab stuff and flee!"

"After a lot of persuasion, Vice City Lord Ma, seeing that we were unwilling to hand over our cultivation resources, started getting agitated. That’s when Vice City Lord Yao arrived, saying there was no need to worry about the beast tide anymore."

"A Supreme Power slew the Four Great Demon Kings with a single sword strike, killing tens, if not hundreds of thousands of the Demon Race, directly resolving the source of the beast tide."

"At first, Ma still said Vice City Lord Yao shouldn’t spread false military information and shake the army’s morale. But once he led a team out of the city and returned, he was utterly demoralized, talking about how it couldn’t be possible, and he was also seriously injured, hurt by the residual Sword Qi."

The apprentice chimed in longingly, "I also heard that the City Lord himself inspected the situation and said that someone at the peak of Sword Dao Supreme made their move."

"Sword Dao Supreme, if I ever get the chance to meet this Sword Dao Supreme, my life would not be in vain."

Lu Yang served four grilled rabbit legs and joked, "What’s so great about a Sword Dao Supreme?"

The apprentice said with a chuckle, "Daoist Lu, you wouldn’t know, but what if the Sword Dao Supreme took a liking to me and passed me a few sword techniques? Then I could walk sideways through Muxue City."

Murong Grandpa took a bite of grilled rabbit leg, his eyes lit up, "Hey, Little Lu, your cooking skills are impressive. You could open a shop with this—In Muxue City, I’ve eaten barbecue for nearly a hundred years, and none is better than yours!"

"You’re exaggerating, exaggerating."
