Ma Family estate.

Ever since Vice City Lord Ma returned home, he had secluded himself, not even meeting his own family.

Vice City Lord Ma sat cross-legged on a straw mat, eyes closed, gritting his teeth, his hands cupped, as beads of sweat trickled down from his forehead, across his chin, down his cheeks, and dropped onto the ground.

The Sword Qi of the Sword Dao Supreme remained in his body, and he tried various methods to expel it quickly but could only wear it down bit by bit.

But that was not his concern. He suddenly opened his eyes, murmuring to himself, "This can’t be, this can’t be..."

"What can’t be?" A weathered voice resounded in Vice City Lord Ma’s ear.

"Who is there?"

Vice City Lord Ma tensed up. This was his cultivation place, absolutely safe; even the City Lord couldn’t just barge in.

"How is it, still have a trace of my Sword Qi inside you and don’t recognize me?"

Vice City Lord Ma’s pupils dilated, his voice filled with agitation, "It’s you, no, it’s You!"

It was the Supreme Sword Master who had slain the Four Great Demon Kings with a single sword strike!

"Vice City Lord Ma thinks something is impossible? Is it that you thought the beast swarm that was supposed to attack the city was halted by me?"

Vice City Lord Ma felt the Sword Master’s oppressive presence and fell to his knees with a thud, beads of sweat the size of soybeans forming on his forehead.

"No, that’s not what I mean," Vice City Lord Ma stammered.

Sword Master withdrew his oppressive presence, noticing Vice City Lord Ma was also a Sword Cultivator. Faced with an overwhelming Sword Cultivator’s pressure, it would be impossible for him to lie.

"I... I never imagined a Sword Cultivator could cultivate to such a level," Vice City Lord Ma said bitterly. As a Sword Cultivator, he knew all too well the chasm between him and the Supreme Sword Master.

Yet he refused to accept this, recklessly touching the Sword Qi left in the Great Demon King’s body, sustaining heavy injuries.

He realized that there was an insurmountable chasm between himself and a true Sword Cultivator, and he would never be able to reach across it in this lifetime, plunging into despair.

Sword Master sneered, "As a Sword Cultivator, yet impure in thought, facing the beast swarm you only thought of abandoning the city, spineless. Yet you aspire to climb to the pinnacle of Sword Dao, laughable."

"In your life, have you ever wielded your sword against someone more powerful than yourself?"

Vice City Lord Ma felt as if struck by lightning.

The Sword Master withdrew the Sword Qi from Vice City Lord Ma’s body and vanished.

Lu Yang appeared outside the Ma Family estate, shaking his head, "It seems he has nothing to do with the beast swarm incident."

Chapter 1163: Chapter 1162: Why Are There So Many Problematic Students?

When the people of Muxue City learned that a Supreme Expert had helped them fend off the beast tide, sparing the city from disaster without any casualties, everyone was very pleased.

But then, the more enterprising cultivators started eyeing the corpses of the demon beasts.

These demon beasts were all at least at the Foundation Establishment Stage, and selling just one could bring in a large number of spirit stones.

However, a very realistic problem soon presented itself—the demon beasts were indeed dealt with by the Supreme Expert, but the Supreme Expert’s Sword Qi also remained within the bodies of the beasts.

Touching the Sword Qi was a lesson already learned by Vice City Lord Ma.

Now, more than a month had passed since the disaster of the beast tide, and the Sword Qi still lingered in the demon beasts’ bodies, almost unchanged.

The cultivators of Muxue City sighed, it seemed that only time could wear down the Sword Qi.

At this moment, the Supreme Sword Master was methodically teaching the children the Tiger Roar Fist.

"Very good, very good, having experienced real combat really makes a difference. As usual, next we’ll start sparring in groups."

Lu Yang was very satisfied with the students’ progress in cultivating the Tiger Roar Fist. Ever since they had fought desperately against that second-level Qi Refinement lone wolf, their boldness had greatly increased.

While mastering the techniques of the Fist was important, boldness was also a crucial factor.

Take Meng Jingzhou for example, Meng Jingzhou was full of vigor, making rapid progress in Fist techniques day by day, to a point where even Lu Yang couldn’t keep up with him.

These students, if placed in the outside world, could also be revered as Great Martial Masters, standing out among ordinary people. However, the students had no concept of their own strength and didn’t know how strong they were.

Their exclamations interrupted Lu Yang’s thoughts.

"Su Yuan actually won?"

"Isn’t he the least talented among us, losing every single time?"

"This is his first win, right?"

"Although Gao Yifan’s strength is below average, he shouldn’t lose to Su Yuan."

Listening to the students’ discussions, Lu Yang roughly understood what had happened—Su Yuan, who had always been at the bottom in terms of talent, had won in this group sparring session.

He had noticed this kid Su Yuan; he was very hardworking, but his talent was indeed very poor.

It was said that he was an orphan, having survived by wandering in his early years. Perhaps it was during that time that he depleted his health, and without cultivator parents like Gong Che, naturally, his foundation was much weaker.

"Su Yuan won, not bad, not bad. It looks like the private training was not in vain." Lu Yang led the applause, always advocating for encouraging education.

"Teacher, I don’t even know what happened just now, it just happened out of the blue," Su Yuan said, feeling embarrassed.

"Bullshit, it was clearly because I was careless!" Gao Yifan angrily said. He could lose to anyone, but losing to Su Yuan, who was the least talented, was too humiliating!

Lu Yang watched the two students with interest: "Is that so? Why don’t you two spar again?"

"Old Gao, are you up for it?"

"Let’s go!"

As the roar of the Tiger sounded, Su Yuan and Gao Yifan began their second round of sparring. It was clear that Su Yuan was at a disadvantage, something all the other students could see.

Suddenly, Su Yuan changed his fist into a claw, reaching for Gao Yifan. Gao Yifan, caught off guard and unsure how to respond, could only retreat.

Su Yuan quickly advanced, launching a rapid punch that broke through Gao Yifan’s defense and knocked him to the ground.

"Su Yuan won again!"

The students exclaimed in surprise. If the first win was an accident, then the second win was a demonstration of true skill.

"Not bad, you’ve indeed improved. But how did you think of changing from fist to claw just now?" Lu Yang asked. That move was the essence of the Tiger Roar Fist, something that couldn’t be explicitly taught but had to be realized intuitively—Su Yuan had seemingly grasped it.

"I just felt it should be done that way."

"Looks like your efforts have paid off. That’s all for today’s lesson," Lu Yang clapped his hands.

...

After the class, Su Yuan looked panicked and hurried back to his thatched house to confront the other voice that had appeared in his mind.

"Who are you, and why won’t you let me tell Teacher Lu the truth!"

Su Yuan demanded. While he was sparring with Gao Yifan, a voice suddenly appeared in his mind, instructing him on his moves.

He was no match for Gao Yifan, but by following the voice’s commands, he won against Gao Yifan twice in succession.

When Lu Yang asked him why he made those moves, he had intended to tell his teacher about the voice in his mind, but the voice stopped him from doing so.

For some reason, that voice made him feel deeply convinced.

"Are you hiding something guilty, that you don’t want me to speak about it!"

"You are naive and do not understand the perils of human nature. My existence is a great secret, and also your opportunity. I have never heard of anyone revealing their opportunities."

"With my help, mastering Tiger Roar Fist and defeating Shi Yi and Gong Che will be effortless."

"But you should improve gradually; rapid changes might attract the attention of those with intentions," the voice said, sounding genuinely considerate for Su Yuan.

However, Su Yuan still didn’t trust the voice and asked cautiously, "Who are you, and why are you inside my body!"

"Who am I?" The voice paused when questioned about its identity, sounding melancholic, "I don’t know who I am either. Maybe someday, you can help me find the answer."

"Really, that sounds quite mysterious." Suddenly, a new voice chimed in, and Su Yuan was delighted.

"Teacher Lu!"

Surprisingly, Teacher Lu had appeared in his home without him knowing.

Lu Yang displayed a mentor-like smile, "I’ve come for a home visit. I hope I’m not interrupting anything?"

The voice did not appear again.

"Come on, no need to hide, I heard everything you both were talking about."

The voice still did not emerge.

Lu Yang waited patiently, gazing at Su Yuan, until finally, the voice couldn’t maintain its composure and spoke with an undertone of threat.

"Kid, though I can’t recall my past, I remember that I was a Combined Great Ability before my death. You, a mere Foundation Establishment Stage cultivator, have no business delving into it!"

Although it was a threat, the voice didn’t emit a convincing aura.

"Combined Great Ability, huh? That does sound strong." Lu Yang sat down and gestured for Su Yuan to sit as well.

Lu Yang then took out two leaves, one for each of them.

"Is this, is this Enlightenment Tea?!" the voice was a bit shocked, surprised that something like this couldn’t be offered by a Foundation Establishment Stage Cultivator.

Who exactly is he!

Lu Yang shook his head, realizing the other couldn’t even recognize that the leaves came from the Enlightenment Tea Tree King.

But it didn’t matter. A senior was still a senior, deserving of respect regardless of their awareness.

He leaned back in his chair, crossed his arms, and scrutinized Su Yuan.

"If I’m not mistaken, senior has been residing in Su Yuan for about a decade, right? Was it because I took Su Yuan out to hunt Demon Beasts that you were awoken, or was it the Yang Qi from the Tiger Roar Fist that stimulated you?"

The voice continued to be silent for a while before finally saying, "The Tiger Roar Fist you taught is not ordinary."

If there were outsiders present, they would realize that Lu Yang was not using Spiritual Sense to talk in the spiritual space; it was a very normal verbal conversation, while the voice spoke using Su Yuan’s body.

Chapter 1164: Chapter 163 The Number One Person with Swordsmanship Talent in the Extreme Northern Lands

Listening to Lu Yang speaking to the mysterious voice, Su Yuan felt uneasy. Seizing the moment when no one paid attention to him, he secretly drank a sip of Enlightenment Tea, and immediately felt his limbs and body lighten up as if he didn’t exist, making every movement exceptionally easy.

"This, this is..."

The voice was astonished; throughout his life, he had drunk Enlightenment Tea countless times, but never had a batch been so powerful.

What year’s Enlightenment Tea is this?

There shouldn’t be tea of such caliber in the Extreme Northern Lands. Moreover, what was the identity of the person who could procure such tea effortlessly?

"Exactly who are you?" the voice toned down its arrogance, realizing that Lu Yang’s origins far exceeded its imagination, most likely belonging to someone of equal stature during its life, or perhaps even a more powerful being.

The only beings more powerful would be those in the Transcendance Tribulation Stage.

"When asking someone’s identity, you should introduce yourself first."

The voice sighed deeply, "What you said is very true, but I really have forgotten my identity."

Lu Yang narrowed his eyes slightly, "Then what do you remember?"

"I am a cultivator from the Extreme Northern Lands at the Integration Peak, having faced a great catastrophe, I intended to possess the body of a frozen beggar in the city. Unexpectedly, after possessing it, I fell into a deep sleep, and the little beggar came back to life."

Hearing this, Su Yuan was quite shocked, "That little beggar..."

"Is you."

Su Yuan looked dazed; his childhood memories were very vague and he couldn’t remember what had happened.

"Faced a great catastrophe, what catastrophe?" Lu Yang stroked his chin, curious about the event itself.

"I can’t remember clearly, only that it was an enemy so powerful that it couldn’t be defeated."

The enemy that forced an Integration Peak cultivator to flee by possession was either on par with his own master’s capability or had to be a Pass Tribulation Cultivator.

"Su Yuan, since nothing major is happening at your home, your teacher is relieved." Lu Yang couldn’t obtain more information and prepared to leave.

Su Yuan exclaimed in surprise. Was this really considered nothing major at home?

"Let’s stop here," Lu Yang advised before leaving, "That voice won’t harm you, but don’t take everything he says at face value. He himself just said that you lack experience and don’t understand the dangers of human hearts. You should still take precautions."

"You!" The voice seemed somewhat angry.

Lu Yang pretended not to hear and left Su Yuan’s house.

"Sir, a roasted sweet potato please." On his way back, Lu Yang rubbed his ears and reddened them, pretending to look as cold as the passersby.

"I didn’t notice this before, but Su Yuan’s soul is quite strong," Lu Yang said while eating the sweet potato.

He gently peeled off the crispy skin to reveal the enticingly glossy, orange-yellow flesh inside. The steam slowly rose, condensing into tiny dewdrops in the cold air, mingling with the falling snow, covering Lu Yang’s face. Taking a bite, the soft, glutinous, sweetly fragrant texture enveloped his taste buds.

Su Yuan’s soul had reached Integration Peak, a level no cultivator in Muxue City could discern unless Lu Yang’s own soul fluctuation was at the Transcendance Tribulation Stage; otherwise, the hints were unnoticeable.

"It’s fine, it’s just at the Integration Realm." In the Spiritual Space, Immortal Fairy constructed a semicircular small house out of snow, lazily lying inside, not feeling the cold at all.

"It’s definitely a split personality."

Su Yuan didn’t know that if one were to possess another, he would, just like Lu Yang, engage in conversation with Immortal Fairy in the Spiritual Space using Su Yuan’s body the entire time.

That is to say, that voice was actually Su Yuan as well.

There was only one soul within Su Yuan’s body to corroborate this conclusion.

According to Lu Yang’s conjecture, it was ten years ago that the voice fought a great battle and, upon losing, possessed the body of a deceased beggar in Muxue City.

Whether it was because the voice was gravely injured, or because the beggar’s body was too weak, the possession encountered a mishap; the voice fell into a deep slumber and also lost its memories, splitting off a sliver of soul to become the new beggar, who was Su Yuan.

Now, Su Yuan was cultivating Tiger Roar Fist, and the masculine energy it generated had awakened that voice.

From their brief exchange, the voice had not realized that Su Yuan was another personality of his.

Perhaps the voice would continually tempt Su Yuan, persuading him to accept its power and thus take control of Su Yuan’s body, or maybe Su Yuan would resist the temptation and gain the power of the voice.

The final outcome would depend on Su Yuan’s own choices.

...

"Did you hear? Xue Shilou is coming to our Muxue City." During the break in the middle of class, students gathered together, speaking in hushed tones and gesticulating continuously, their eyebrows twitching; it was evident that Xue Shilou held much significance to them.

"That hero Xue Shilou who punishes the wicked and routes out evil?" Gong Che asked excitedly; Xue Shilou’s reputation for upholding justice was well known across the Extreme Northern Lands, and what young person wouldn’t admire him?

He was the number one in Swordmanship Talent in the Extreme Northern Lands, a title alone that could attract countless admirers.

"Yes, that’s him. It’s said he was drawn here by the Sword Qi of that unparalleled Sword Cultivator during the beast tide, wanting to observe those Sword Qi."

"I also heard he was once an opponent of Talent Lu, Lu Yang, is that true?" Shi Yi, very excited, could hardly stay seated.

"It is true. They were opponents at the Sword Inquiry Ceremony held in the Sword Tower. It’s said that among the opponents Talent Lu encountered during that ceremony, aside from Ming Lou, the successor of the Sword Tower, Xue Shilou was the strongest," Gong Che said, his family being cultivators knew more than the average person.

A duel between such formidable opponents was always a captivating topic, especially involving talents like Xue Shilou and Lu Yang, who were renowned throughout both the Extreme Northern Lands and the entire Cultivation World.

Ah, Xue Shilou, Lu Yang was briefly stunned when he heard this name; after hearing Gong Che elaborating, he then recalled who Xue Shilou was.

Indeed, Xue Shilou was a formidable opponent he encountered at the Sword Inquiry Ceremony; against other competitors he would only execute a single sword strike, but to defeat Xue Shilou, he had unleashed three full strikes.

"Alright, stop discussing, class is starting," Lu Yang shouted, the students reluctantly responded, engrossed as they were in their discussions.

The door of the Martial Arts Hall suddenly burst open with a whoosh of cold wind rushing inward, and a swordsman in black appeared, quickly shutting the door.

Xue Shilou sighed in relief; someone had inadvertently recognized him, causing the whole street to swarm with people, and unfamiliar with the place, he could only hide somewhere arbitrarily.

As Xue Shilou turned around, he noticed thirty-three students and sixty-six eyes staring directly at him, which made him somewhat embarrassed.

Suddenly, he noticed the teaching instructor, backed away several steps, nearly tripping over the threshold: "Is it you?"

He hurriedly looked up at the signboard overhead—yes, this was the Martial Arts Hall, not the City Lord’s residence.

"Focus, this gentleman is a friend of the instructor," Lu Yang said calmly, then glanced again at Xue Shilou.

"Keep quiet, don’t interrupt my class; we can talk after it’s over." fɾeewebnovel.co๓

Xue Shilou nodded woodenly.

Chapter 1165: Chapter 1164: A New Teacher Added

"Goodbye, Teacher Lu."

After class, the students left in small groups, walking home together. Each of them glanced at the corner, where a black-clothed swordsman with seemingly no presence sat quietly as they passed the gate.

After all the students had left, Xue Shilou finally spoke.

"You seem quite amused, Daoist Lu," Xue Shilou managed to say after holding it in for so long.

Sword cultivators typically aren’t talkative, with Daoist Buyu and Lu Yang being the two exceptions.

Xue Shilou really didn’t know what to say. Teaching a group of students fist techniques, it seemed they were unaware of Lu Yang’s identity; otherwise, their reaction wouldn’t have been so indifferent.

Why teach them? Teach me! How much does your martial arts hall charge per lesson? I want to sign up!

"Just experiencing life. I’ve heard you have a pretty good reputation in the Extreme Northern Lands, Snow Daoist," Lu Yang teased.

During the Sword Inquiry Ceremony at the Sword Tower, Xue Shilou was somewhat famous in the Extreme Northern Lands. Not seeing him for several years, Lu Yang didn’t expect his fame in the Extreme Northern Lands to have grown so much that he could carry the title of the one with the best swordmanship talent in the Extreme Northern Lands.

With cultivation level at the late stage of Spirit Transformation, his talent indeed allowed him to walk sideways in the Extreme Northern Lands. Even if he encountered a Great Demon King, he could escape unscathed.

"It’s all just hype from the people. I’m nowhere near as renowned as Daoist Lu," Xue Shilou admitted. He knew his fame only extended to the Extreme Northern Lands and beyond that, no one would recognize him.

But Lu Yang was different. It wouldn’t be an exaggeration to say that his name was known across the world.

It was as if Xue Shilou finally found a topic he could talk about and took the initiative to engage in conversation: "The Sword Qi on the Frost Elephant Demon King’s corpse is truly awe-inspiring. Even if I cultivated to the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, I would have no confidence in unleashing a sword strike to match it."

"I never expected such a marvel in our Extreme Northern Lands. A single sword strike vanquished the Four Great Demon Kings so cleanly and efficiently. The Sword Qi lingers on without fading. I’ve heard that the sword cultivator Vice City Lord of Muxue City, upon witnessing that Sword Qi, was so ashamed that he nearly mutilated himself and almost gave up on swordsmanship."

"I have a premonition that the key to my breakthrough to the Void Refinement Stage lies here in Muxue City. Observing this Sword Qi and comprehending a fraction of its mysteries will surely elevate my Sword Intent to a new level."

"Speaking of which, why is Daoist Lu in Muxue City? Are you also here to observe that Sword Qi?"

"Oh, that Sword Qi was left by me."

"Cough cough—" Xue Shilou suddenly choked and coughed violently, his cheeks flushing with embarrassment, almost coughing out his lungs.

"You?!"

Lu Yang was somewhat surprised by Xue Shilou’s reaction, "Didn’t you know, Snow Daoist, I’m currently at the Void Refinement Stage, spending my days here amidst the mortal realm."

"You’re at the Void Refinement Stage?!"

Xue Shilou coughed even more violently. At the time of the Sword Inquiry Ceremony, he was at the mid-stage of Transforming Spirit while Lu Yang was at the initial stage. Then he had been forcefully taken across the border by his Senior Brother and captured by Laurel Fairy Palace, where with their help, he truly awakened his Snow Emperor Bloodline. After diving into intensive cultivation in the Extreme Northern Lands, how could it be that Lu Yang’s cultivation progress had surpassed his own?

"That’s wrong, though. Even if you’re at the Void Refinement Stage, the realm fluctuation reaching the Body Integration Realm wouldn’t be enough to deliver such a strike!"

"Oh, you’re talking about that. It happened when I accidentally triggered an unprecedented Thunder Tribulation during my breakthrough to the Void Refinement Stage, which made my Void Refinement Stage somewhat different from others. My realm fluctuation ranges from the Qi Cultivation Stage to the Pass Tribulation Stage."

Xue Shilou was completely numb by this point. He felt he shouldn’t have come to Muxue City.

Even if he thought he had a strong Dao heart, it couldn’t withstand such continual blows.

"Will Daoist Lu be staying in Muxue City for a while?"

"Given the constant fluctuation in my realm, it could be quite dangerous to go to other places. I’ll be staying at this martial arts hall for the time being."

"Is the martial arts hall still recruiting? Can I stay here?" Xue Shilou asked excitedly.

He had originally planned to stay in Muxue City for some time to learn from the Sword Qi on the Frost Elephant Demon King’s corpse. Now that Lu Yang was here, there was no need to look elsewhere.

"You’ll have to ask Master Murong about that. Oh, Master Murong is the Sect Leader of the Tiger Roar Sect."

Lu Yang realized what Xue Shilou meant, but he didn’t mind; after all, it didn’t matter whom he taught.

Xue Shilou straightened his clothes and went to visit the Sect Leader of the Tiger Roar Sect.

He wasn’t afraid of Murong You recognizing him. Although he was well-known, few people in the Extreme Northern Lands had actually seen his true face. He was once recognized by accident when someone shouted in excitement upon seeing him, causing a rumor-fueled chase after him.

Of course, the most important reason was that he did not know the Disguise Skill.

Sword Cultivators are straightforward in their actions, how could they engage in activities that require hiding and sneaking around?

Master Murong’s Abode was located in the deepest part of the Martial Arts Hall’s backyard. Lu Yang brought Xue Shilou over: "Is Master Murong here?"

"Come in."

Lu Yang and Xue Shilou entered.

"Little Lu, who is this?"

"Hello, Master Murong, my surname is Xue. I’m a friend of Teacher Lu and would like to teach at our Martial Arts Hall."

Murong You was greatly surprised: "You’re Little Lu’s friend? Little Lu, has your memory recovered?"

"...It has recovered a part."

Murong You, wise with age, instantly understood the situation. Little Lu’s memory had only partially recovered, and he couldn’t be overstimulated. He needed to recover gradually. To take care of Little Lu, his friend decided to stay at his Martial Arts Hall for a while.

"What is Teacher Xue’s Cultivation Level, and what does he want to teach?"

"Foundation...Foundation Establishment Early Stage. I have some understanding of Swordsmanship and can teach them that."

"We can’t do Swordsmanship." Master Murong shook his head, "Swords are expensive after all. Most students here come from families with not much money, they can’t even afford swords, so learning Swordsmanship would be useless to them."

Xue Shilou turned to Lu Yang for help, what else could he teach if not Swordsmanship? Was he supposed to teach the students how to maintain their composure in battle so that their clothes wouldn’t get stained with blood?

Lu Yang stepped forward to speak for Xue Shilou: "He can teach the Rake Skill, the Shovel Skill."

"Rake Skill, Shovel Skill? That could work." Murong You’s eyes brightened, not expecting Little Lu’s friend to be so versatile.

Rakes and shovels are farming tools but could also be used as weapons in critical moments. However, such weapons are quite rare, and very few in Muxue City know how to wield them.

Do I know the Rake Skill and Shovel Skill?

Xue Shilou pondered and indeed felt competent; as the saying goes, all paths lead to the same goal in the great Dao. Being devoted to the art of the sword, he had cultivated to the Spirit Transformation Stage, which allowed him to have an understanding of other weapons through analogy. Teaching a group of students would be more than manageable.

"As for the monthly salary, how about five Spirit Stones per month?"

"That’s fine." Xue Shilou didn’t care much about making money.

"Then you can live next to Little Lu."

Now officially a teacher, Xue Shilou could legitimately stay at the Martial Arts Hall and ask Lu Yang for guidance in Swordsmanship.

"Fellow Daoist Lu Yang, I have some doubts about Swordsmanship..."

Lu Yang gave Xue Shilou a look: "What Swordsmanship? Do you know the Rake Skill, the Shovel Skill? Go practice on your own first, otherwise, how will you teach the students tomorrow?"

"Oh."

On his first day at Tiger Roar Martial Arts Hall, Xue Shilou learned how to use a hooked rake and a shovel.

Chapter 1166: Chapter 1165: Ice Flood Dragon Clan

In the dead of night, Xue Shilou closed his eyes and focused, treating the rake in his hand as if it were his sword. Suddenly opening his eyes, he swung it with the force of a gale, every move executed with precision and method.

Even the seasoned masters of rake skill in Muxue City, upon seeing Xue Shilou’s actions, would have to admit their respect, for Xue Shilou wielded it much stronger than they.

But Xue Shilou felt it still wasn’t enough.

Not fast enough, not fast enough, it needed to be faster, even faster!

The rake in his hand left behind trails of illusory shadows as he swung, and eventually, he was so tired he was huffing and puffing, propping himself up with the rake to barely stand, maintaining the poise of a sword cultivator.

Daoist Lu had him practice the rake skill, which must contain deeper meaning, certainly not as simple as merely teaching the students the rake skill.

Xue Shilou stared at the rake handle, now imprinted by his grip, letting his mind wander.

The rake, the rake... A flash of insight struck Xue Shilou, and he suddenly understood.

Of course, how had he not realized this point before - when swinging the rake, its nine teeth would attack the enemy simultaneously, which perfectly embodies the principle of "One Sword Becomes Ten Thousand" and "Ten Thousand Swords Returning to Origin".

If the rake could simultaneously encapsulate these two completely opposite sword skills, could it be that these two sword skills shared something in common?

Daoist Lu was definitely hinting at this!

With this realization, Xue Shilou’s thoughts flowed smoothly, and he was at Lu Yang’s door first thing in the morning to express his gratitude.

"Thank you, Daoist Lu, for your guidance. I’ve had an epiphany."

"..."

Last night, Lu Yang had spent a long evening accompanying Fairy Eternity, and now his mind was still in a haze, not, what epiphany did you have?

"Good, having an epiphany is what matters."

At Hunter Shi’s home.

Shi Yi had a very long dream, in which he saw himself falling into an ice hole and being swept away by a rapid undercurrent.

Logically speaking, falling into an undercurrent, he should have felt exceedingly cold, but instead, he felt abnormally warm, as if he was born to live there.

Shi Yi suddenly opened his eyes, only to find himself standing in the icy snow outside the house, bare-chested yet not feeling cold at all.

"Hmm? How did I end up here?"

Shi Yi felt an itch on his arm and scratched it subconsciously, only to realize something was amiss. Looking down, he saw a few ice crystal-like snake scales had grown on his arm!

"Dad, look at my arm!" Shi Yi quickly ran into the house to find his father, a renowned hunter who, despite being an ordinary human, had trapped and killed Demon Beasts of the Qi Refinement first and second layers, truly formidable.

Hunter Shi was splitting firewood when he saw the snake scales on Shi Yi’s arm; the axe dropped from his hands and thudded into the snow.

"Ah, so you’ve finally awakened?"

"Dad, what’s happening to me, you know, don’t you?" Seeing his father’s reaction, how could Shi Yi not realize that his father had long anticipated this day?

"Does this have something to do with my mother?"

Shi Yi had never met his mother, and though his father said she died in childbirth, Shi Yi always felt that his father’s tone was off, as if there was more to the story.

Hunter Shi beckoned Shi Yi inside to put on some clothes, and the father and son sat next to the table.

"I originally wanted to take this secret to my grave, but since you’ve inherited your mother’s bloodline, there’s no need to conceal it any longer." Hunter Shi took a puff of tobacco, reminiscing about the past twenty years.

"Twenty years ago, I was out hunting and came across a woman in the snow, beautiful as a fairy. Seeing that the fairy was gravely injured, I brought her back."

"When the fairy awoke, she was very hostile towards me, but gradually, as we interacted more, her attitude softened, and she no longer bore any hostility towards me."

"The fairy told me she was in the Void Refinement Stage, which made her realm very unstable, and she had been attacked while out on her practice, resulting in her severe injuries and coma."

"You must have guessed the fairy’s identity by now; she was your mother, Bing Wu."

"Later, we fell in love, and you were born, our family of three living a sweet life."

"Unfortunately, the happiness was short-lived. Your mother’s clan came for her, intending to take her away and kill both me and you."

"That was when I learned that your mother wasn’t from the Human race, but from the Ice Flood Dragon Clan."

"That legendary clan capable of creating ice with their breath, the Ice Flood Dragon Clan?" Shi Yi’s body trembled with the revelation.

"Yes, and your mother was the Holy Daughter of the Ice Flood Dragon Clan, the most likely to transform into a dragon in a thousand years."

"She married me and gave birth to you, which was a violation of our clan’s taboo, a sign of bad omen."

"It was your mother who, with death staring her in the face, forced the Ice Flood Dragon Clan to spare the lives of us both."

"The scales on your arm are the symbol of the Ice Flood Dragon Clan."

"I thought you would never awaken the Ice Flood Dragon Bloodline and would live a safe and uneventful life. That was also your mother’s wish, but alas, against all odds, you have ultimately awakened the Ice Flood Dragon Bloodline."

Shi Yi clenched his fists so tightly his nails dug into his flesh, whitening his knuckles, "Where is my mother?"

The hunter sighed, "Probably detained in the Ice Flood Dragon Clan’s forbidden grounds."

"Before she left, your mother instructed me to tell you to never entertain the thought of rescuing her. Even the high officials of Muxue City must yield three steps when they encounter the Ice Flood Dragon Clan. How can you possibly contend with them?"

Shi Yi fell silent, his heart bleeding, feeling his own weakness.

"Alright, it’s getting late. Go to class."

The Ice Flood Dragon Clan had an ice sculpture, a statue of an ice dragon, carved so lifelike that suddenly one of the dragon’s scales started to shimmer. The guardians of the sculpture immediately reported the situation to the Clan Leader.

The Ice Flood Dragon Clan Leader was attempting to persuade a stunning woman, "Bing Wu, just marry my son obediently. The union of the strongest bloodlines might mean that your child is born with Dragon’s Blood."

Chapter 1167: Chapter 1166: This Door is Not Sturdy at All

Old Ma scraped the frozen ground with its hooves, revealing the ice-crystal-covered wild grass, took a bite, and shook its tail.

The grass from the Extreme Northern Lands really did taste different.

When class began, Lu Yang introduced Master Meng, the boxing master. During the break, Meng Jingzhou pulled Lu Yang aside.

"Are you saying that this Gong Che person has a cold qi in his body and needs my blood to remove it?"

"Right, any problem?"

"Damn it, although the kid had a cold qi before, now he practices Tiger Roar Fist every day, and the cold qi is almost gone. In a few more days, it’ll be completely expelled!"

"It’s just removing it one day earlier."

"And what’s with these students of yours? One has a hint of flood dragon blood awakening in his human bloodline, another is outright a cultivator, and another has scary high spiritual power and always talks to himself."

"You don’t get it. Though we often say the ’general public,’ meaning that ordinary people are very ordinary, in reality, how can people be exactly the same? These students are just ordinary people with some quirks; don’t overthink it."

Meng Jingzhou was momentarily dazed, feeling there was some truth in Old Lu’s words: "Are these your insights from transcending the mundane world?"

"That’s just a line I made up on the spot to fool you."

Chapter 1171: Chapter 1170 What Kind of Door is This?!

Today was a rare day off, with no need to attend private school or practice fist techniques at the Martial Arts Hall. Gong Che and Shi Yi had arranged to go out and stroll through the streets.

"You just call me out to hang out, but what exactly are we going to do?"

Shi Yi rolled his eyes, feeling that Gong Che had been unusually excited lately. Not only was he active during lessons, but he couldn’t sit still during his days off either, waking him up early in the morning.

Ever since his mother returned from the Ice Flood Dragon Clan, his father and mother had been inseparable and saccharine, leaving him feeling somewhat superfluous.

Perhaps that was why, under the guise of "friends are hard to come by, you should go out and play," his parents had shooed him out of the house.

"Why not think about it on the way? After all, you have nothing else to do at home, right?"

"How about this, I’ll treat you to lunch today!" Gong Che said generously.

"What’s the good news that’s put you in such a good mood?" Shi Yi asked, looking at Gong Che with suspicion.

Gong Che had been waiting for Shi Yi to ask this question, and now it had finally come.

"I can finally live past sixteen."

"What do you mean by that?"

"I’m just telling you this—you better not tell anyone else."

"Go on."

Gong Che spoke seriously, "Actually, I’m an orphan who was picked up. I was born with a cold qi in my body, meaning I wouldn’t live past sixteen. I learned all of this by overhearing my parents talking when I went to the bathroom at night."

"They thought I didn’t know, but actually, I knew everything."

Shi Yi was stunned for a moment, not expecting Gong Che to have such a tragic past. "So what about you now..."

"To live past sixteen, I must get rid of the cold qi in my body. My parents tried all kinds of methods to no avail, except for Tiger Roar Fist, which had only a slight effect, but it couldn’t change my fate."

"Until recently, when Teacher Lu started teaching us Tiger Roar Fist, the cold qi in my body began to truly dissipate, and just five days ago, it completely vanished!"

"Does that mean you can keep on living now?" Shi Yi finally understood why Gong Che had been so happy lately. Knowing this, he too was happy for Gong Che.

Shi Yi felt that Gong Che confiding his secret was a sign of trust and that he too should share his own secret.

"Actually, my veins carry the bloodline of the Ice Flood Dragon Clan..."

Shi Yi revealed everything he knew.

He rolled up his sleeves to show the ice crystal-like Flood Dragon scales on his arm.

"No wonder I could never beat you no matter how much I practiced, so you’ve awakened your bloodline." Gong Che suddenly realized why he’d been surpassed. Initially, he was the number one in the fist technique class; then, after Teacher Lu arrived, Shi Yi surpassed him. After learning from Teacher Lu, he surpassed Shi Yi again, but then somehow, Shi Yi overtook him once more.

"But why did your mom tell you to thank Teacher Lu and even send a banner of appreciation?"

Shi Yi shook his head, "I don’t know, my mom didn’t explain."

"Hey boss, give us two baked sweet potatoes, he’s paying." As they passed by a baked sweet potato stall, Shi Yi spoke.

With baked sweet potatoes in hand, and unstoppable smiles on their faces, Shi Yi continued the previous conversation.

"Enough about me, what about you? Have you ever thought about finding your biological parents?"

Gong Che took a bite of his baked sweet potato and mumbled unclearly, "At first, when I found out I was adopted, I thought about looking for my biological parents. But then I realized it’s better to treasure what I have now than to chase parents without any leads."

"Perhaps when I meet my biological parents, I’ll ask them why they abandoned me in the snow and left me to fend for myself."

Suddenly, the two halted their steps as a youth who bore a seven-point resemblance to Gong Che appeared before them.

The youth’s gloomy eyes were filled with a thick murderous intent, and he flashed a sinister smile.

"Wu Ma, I didn’t expect you to still be alive."

Gong Che was taken aback. Wu Ma? Is that me?

The youth stepped closer, "The most failed experiment, abandoned by mom and dad for not being able to endure the Mystic Heavenly Cold Qi, not only survived until now but also dissipated the cold qi within?"

"I thought I had killed Zi Shu, Chou Niu, Mao Tu, and possessed the qualification to cultivate the Xuantian Scripture. But to think, you’re still alive!"

"The Xuantian Scripture is a supreme cultivation technique, with strict conditions for practice. Only those who endured the Mystic Heavenly Cold Qi in their youth are qualified to practice it, and it can only be cultivated when there is one eligible person."

"Now that both of us are qualified, I can’t cultivate it while you’re alive!"

"Remember my name before you die. I am Yin Hu!"

Yin Hu made a move as if to pounce, but Shi Yi quickly stepped forward and pinned the leaping Yin Hu to the ground.

Yin Hu made several attempts to rise, only to find that Shi Yi’s strength was astonishing, and he couldn’t get up at all!

Who was this person?!

"Your brother?" Shi Yi asked Gong Che, who looked utterly bewildered.

"I don’t know him, but listening to all his muttering just now, he doesn’t sound like a good person."

Yin Hu raised his head, staring fixedly at Gong Che. Rather than tiger eyes, they seemed more like viper slits. "Wu Ma, if you dare, let him go, and let’s see who the stronger successor really is!"

"Okay."

Yin Hu shook free from his restraints and lunged ferociously at Gong Che with claws outstretched, like a tiger descending the mountain, fierce and bloodthirsty!

Roar—

A youthful tiger’s roar erupted, and with two punches, Gong Che left Yin Hu battered and unable to rise from the ground.

Yin Hu’s pupils shook with disbelief; how was the other person more like a tiger than him?

"Is that all?"

Gong Che was stunned; after all the bluster, this guy didn’t put up a fight at all.

However, Gong Che did not let down his guard. He remembered that Teacher Lu had mentioned in class that some opponents, seemingly easy to handle and taken down in one move, might actually be hiding terrifying power within their bodies and rise up to continue fighting.

Gong Che and Shi Yi warily watched Yin Hu lying on the ground, motionless.

Just when the two thought the matter was about to end, a man and a woman with an extraordinary demeanor approached them; one could tell at a glance they were cultivators.

Seeing the man and woman, Yin Hu mustered his last bit of strength to get up from the ground, clutching at the woman’s leg and begging pitifully, "Dad, Mom, please give me another chance, I’ll definitely defeat him!"

The woman looked at Yin Hu with disgust, kicked him away, and then immediately put on a tearful face, looking at Gong Che with pity.

"Child, Mom has finally found you!"

"Stay away!" Gong Che shouted, linking Yin Hu’s nonsense and the woman’s reaction, he roughly guessed the identity of the couple.

They were his own biological parents, and they had given birth to him merely to choose the strongest child to cultivate the inscrutable "Xuantian Scripture"!

"Child, what’s wrong with you, we are your biological parents," the woman called out.

"Why did you abandon me in the first place!"

"Child, you’ve become so strong exactly because Dad and Mom abandoned you, which allowed you to seize the opportunity and achieve today’s success, defeating your worthless brother."

"Perhaps what Dad and Mom did back then was ill-considered, but after all, we are your biological parents, as the saying goes, blood is thicker than water. Is there anything we can’t sit down and talk about?" The woman had a bewitching ability to speak that made one involuntarily believe her.

"Come, child, come to Mom," the woman opened her arms.

Gong Che didn’t even think about it and, grabbing Shi Yi, turned and ran.

"Run!"

"Trying to run?" The man flicked his sleeve, transforming it into an invisible giant hand that reached for Gong Che and Shi Yi.

Unexpectedly, Shi Yi’s body emitted the sound of a Flood Dragon, blocking the invisible hand.

"Pursue!"

The man and woman said through clenched teeth. Although they were Nascent Soul Stage powerhouses, here they were in Muxue City, where too much fanfare could draw the attention of the law enforcers. Pfft—

What kind of door was this?!

Faced with the Divinity Transformation Stage, the man and the woman dared not hold back any longer. They bit their tongues and used a secret technique to transform into a mist of blood to escape.

How could it be that there really were forces from the Ruthless Sect in the Extreme Northern Lands?

Chapter 1172: Chapter 1171: Snow Emperor Bloodline

Chapter 1173: Chapter 1172 Unlucky Thief

In the Extreme Northern Lands, the temperature difference between day and night is vast, with daytime so cold that people are reluctant to reach out their hands, and nights even colder.

As a result, Muxue City had no nightlife. When night fell, every household turned off their lights and went to sleep, leaving the whole city eerily quiet.

A roar erupted, and the entire city could hear Vice City Lord Ma’s furious shouting.

"Who is the scoundrel who dares to steal into my house? You’re courting death!"

A black figure jumped between rooftops, appearing and disappearing, as if he didn’t exist in this space, his movements extremely cunning.

Accompanied by Vice City Lord Ma’s lion-like roar, a bright Sword Qi slashed down, striking the continuously leaping figure.

How could Vice City Lord Ma not be furious; he had recently gained insight into the Sword Dao and had chosen to seclude himself from the outside world. Little did he expect someone to mistake him for being seriously injured and healing, to have the audacity to steal into his house—an outright provocation.

The thief clutched his right arm, a look of resentment on his face. He thought he could evade the sword and leave gracefully, but it turned out that Vice City Lord Ma was not only uninjured but had also improved his swordsmanship, resulting in the thief taking a hit.

"Ma, you wait for me! I’ll not only steal your things, but I’ll also take your daughter away!"

Vice City Lord Ma trembled with anger, ordering a citywide manhunt. In no time, Muxue City was as bright as daytime, lit up throughout.

The thief took an elixir to temporarily stop his wound from worsening. With Muxue City on full alert, an escape was currently out of the question. He needed to find a place to rest first; he would find a way to flee Muxue City later.

He jumped into a courtyard and discovered a beautiful stable where a snow-white steed was swishing its tail and munching grass.

"Is this a Dragon Horse?!"

The thief’s heart leapt with joy; to think that a Dragon Horse from the East Sea would appear in the Extreme Northern Lands, and by the looks of it, a Pure Blood Dragon Horse at that, invaluable.

"If I’m not mistaken, this is the Tiger Roar Sect?"

"It seems the Tiger Roar Sect has struck it rich; I wonder where they got this Dragon Horse from."

"Looks like the cultivation level of the Dragon Horse isn’t too high; otherwise, it would have transformed by now. It’s just perfect for me!"

The thief approached the Dragon Horse with a grin on his face, thinking that getting a Pure Blood Dragon Horse in Muxue City made getting stabbed by that sword worth it.

The Dragon Horse glanced at the thief and continued to eat grass.

With his hands forming a spell-sealing position, the thief whispered an unknown magic skill, trying to control the Dragon Horse with the Beast Taming Technique.

The Beast Taming Mark landed on the Dragon Horse, which had not resisted from the beginning to the end.

"Success."

However, just as the Beast Taming Mark touched the Dragon Horse, the thief’s face drastically changed; there was something strange about this Dragon Horse!

The thief suffered a backlash from the Beast Taming Technique, and his vitality plummeted. He staggered back two steps with a pale face and depleted Qi and Blood.

The previous sword wound that had stopped bleeding intensified, and under the dual burden, his right hand became completely useless!

"What’s that noise?"

Huo Huashen, upon hearing the faint commotion in the backyard, ran over anxiously.

The thief saw that there was no time to leave the Tiger Roar Sect and resorted to using a secret technique to conceal his aura and form.

This was his unique secret technique; whether using the naked eye or Spiritual Sense to search, one couldn’t see him.

"Is there no one?"

Huo Huashen was puzzled; as someone at the Divinity Transformation Stage, he shouldn’t be experiencing auditory hallucinations.

But even when he used his Spiritual Sense, he couldn’t detect anyone—there was only Old Ma grazing in the stables.

"Let’s test it." Huo Huashen flicked his sleeve, releasing a Blood Demon Saber and hacking out countless waves of Sword Qi.

The thief widened his eyes in disbelief; the other party was a Sword Cultivator at the Divinity Transformation Stage?!

If he had not been injured, he wouldn’t have cared about someone at the Divinity Transformation Stage, but with his serious injuries, setting aside the outcome of a fight, it would certainly draw Vice City Lord Ma’s attention.

The Sword Qi slashed into him, and he bit down on his clothes, making no sound, dare not let Huo Huashen discover him.

"So there really is no one."

Huo Huashen let Sword Qi flood the entire backyard and still couldn’t find anyone. He could only conclude that he heard things because he was too excited about being on guard duty.

After Huo Huashen left, the thief showed himself, kneeling on the ground with one hand propping up his body, gasping for breath, sweat continuously beading on his forehead, his consciousness blurry and confused.

This won’t do; he had to find a place to rest, to leave this place. There was something strange about this place; the Tiger Roar Sect was far from simple...

The thief approached a room in the courtyard, outside of which hung a small wooden sword.

As he approached the room, the small wooden sword emitted Sword Qi and immediately repelled him.

The rake teeth were exceptionally sharp, and as the thief collided headfirst with them, several bloody holes were punctured into his head. He struggled on the ground for a moment and soon lay immovable.

"Ah, oh."

Lu Yang and Xue Shilou carried the Carefree Guest’s body, moving it under the tree near the door of Lu Yang’s room.

Fittingly, just beneath the tree were buried the remains of Luo Shi, a Foundation Establishment Stage killer from the Ghost Killing Alliance. Knowing that his body now had for company the formerly strongest Divine Transformation Stage Carefree Guest would probably make him die happy.

"Old Lu, is something happening outside..."

Meng Jingzhou walked out of his room, watching Lu Yang and Xue Shilou carrying an unrecognizable body, one in front and the other behind.

"I didn’t see anything, I’m going back."

"Go back my ass, come help."

"Ugh."

Meng Jingzhou reluctantly picked up the right arm of the Carefree Guest and placed it back onto his body.

Lu Yang pulled out three shovels, and each of them began to dig a hole.

Meng Jingzhou and Xue Shilou, unaccustomed to such rough work, moved awkwardly. In comparison, Lu Yang worked with practiced ease.

Xue Shilou thoughtfully pondered, could this be the real usage of the shovel? Had he been misunderstanding it all along?

Now that he had passed the second round of the trial, it was time to focus completely on creating his own unique moves.

"I see why the tree at your door grows so well; it’s well-nourished," Meng Jingzhou commented as he dug. The method was unique and not easily imitated.

Upon hearing the report from his subordinate, Vice City Lord Ma’s expression turned cold enough to drip water, frightening his subordinate not to even dare breathe.

"The only Divine Transformation Stage Cultivator who could escape me must be the Carefree Guest!"

"Still no clue to that bandit’s whereabouts, damn it, he got away!"

The Carefree Guest’s final words of threat lingered in his mind. Vice City Lord Ma couldn’t always be on guard against the Carefree Guest; raging, he hit the table, "Find him! Dig three feet into the ground if you have to!"

Muxue City was locked down for ten days, the whole city hunting for the Carefree Guest, but found nothing.

Clearly, the soldiers of Muxue City were not strictly executing Vice City Lord Ma’s order to dig three feet into the ground.

...

Soul Cliff.

A rope was tied around a boulder, dangling down to the bottom of Soul Cliff. Su Yuan held the rope tensely, waiting for any signals from the other end.

Suddenly, the rope shook; Su Yuan snapped to attention and quickly pulled up the rope.

Feeling the vibrations along the rope, Su Yuan sensed that the person on the other end was climbing up rapidly.

A figure flashed by, somersaulting several times in the air before landing steadily.

It was Fang Zhige!

"Three days, and you finally came up. If you hadn’t, I would have had to call on Old Lu for help," Zhige said. "How did it go, any gains?"

The usually solemn Fang Zhige unexpectedly showed a cheerful smile, "I passed!"

"That’s great!"

Hearing Fang Zhige’s response, Su Yuan involuntarily thought of the events that had occurred not long ago.

The voice inside him had informed him that by devouring the soul of the Ghost Kill Alliance Leader, he learned of an Ancient Secret Realm known as the Killing Heart Ancient Realm.

The Killing Heart Ancient Realm was an opportunity that allowed the Ghost Kill Alliance Leader to rise early in his career. He passed the first trial in the realm and acquired the incomplete "Killing Heart Scripture," which transformed him into a feared assassin.

He had fled to Muxue City, also hoping to rise again by overcoming subsequent trials in the realm.

The Killing Heart Ancient Realm was located in the deepest part of Soul Cliff.

However, the only way to enter the Killing Heart Ancient Realm was to harbor a killing intent. The voice had tried several times to tempt Su Yuan into killing, but Su Yuan had firmly refused.

Having no other choice, the voice then had Su Yuan contact Fang Zhige, who possessed the necessary killing intent to qualify for entry into the Killing Heart Ancient Realm, agreeing to split any gains fifty-fifty.

After lengthy discussions and thorough preparations with Su Yuan, Fang Zhige finally decided to venture into Soul Cliff.

The voice recognized that Fang Zhige was a cultivator at the Great Perfection of Qi Refinement. If Fang Zhige betrayed them after gaining some benefits, he could control Su Yuan’s body under the guise of saving him.

Fang Zhige had no intention of betraying, however. As per their agreement, he detailed the gains from the Killing Heart Ancient Realm.

"The Killing Heart Ancient Realm seems to be a relic left by an Ancient Killer of great power, who had no descendants or disciples, hence setting up the secret realm, hoping to pass down her legacy."

"The realm comprises three trials. I was fairly lucky to have passed all three."

Though Fang Zhige spoke lightly, Su Yuan could see the fear in his eyes when he mentioned this, indicating the trials were not easy to pass.

"This is the ’Killing Heart Scripture’ that only I can cultivate. I’m keeping this for myself," Fang Zhige said, pulling out an ancient scripture, also the Cultivation Technique practiced by that Ancient Killer.

"Alright."

"Since the Killing Heart Scripture is mine, here’s sixty percent of the Spirit Stones and the other techniques for you."

"I actually obtained one more thing from the Ancient Realm, something I can’t understand, and it wasn’t mentioned in the transmission of memories."

"What is it?"

Fang Zhige unwrapped the package on his back, revealing a three-foot-long ice box.

Only then did Su Yuan notice that Fang Zhige had a package on his back; he hadn’t carried one when he went down.

"This ice box can’t be stored in the Storage Ring and has a seal set on it; I don’t know how to open it." ƒreeωebnovel.ƈom

"However, from the transmitted memories I received, it seems whatever is inside the ice box was very important to the owner of the Ancient Realm."

"Do you know what this is?" Su Yuan asked the voice inside him.

The voice, unusually silent, didn’t know what was inside and was embarrassed to say so.

"Maybe Old Lu has seen many things; how about we ask him when we get back?"

"Let’s go. There’s a parent-teacher meeting soon; we shouldn’t be late," Fang Zhige said, also trusting Old Lu deeply.

...

Facing the combined forces of the Jiuyou Sect and the Yaoyang Sect, the Ruthless Sect’s disciples were either captured or directly subjected to Soul Searches, with extremely efficient operations.

The three Transcendance Tribulation Stage great powers from both sects sat together, sharing the intelligence gathered.

The Chi Sect Leader of the Yaoyang Sect, grimacing, uncertain whether to cry or laugh, said, "The situation is more tricky than we imagined. I didn’t expect that the Ruthless Sect Leader is really in the Extreme Northern Lands, and it seems he is searching for something."

"Just don’t know where he is now; otherwise, we could take the initiative to strike and perhaps resolve this in one fell swoop."

Mu Baiyi took out a piece of freshly obtained intelligence, showing it to the Yaoyang Sect, "I found out that there’s a famous Divine Transformation Stage individual known as the Carefree Guest in the Extreme Northern Lands, a disciple of the Ruthless Sect Leader."

"And the last place the Carefree Guest was seen was in Muxue City."
